‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢

üî¥ ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: Claude ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö / ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô Figma

  4. ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Claude Code ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡πÉ‡∏ô VS Code

Foundations ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î

FoundationDescription
Color SystemColor scale (50-950) + Semantic colors + Light/Dark mode + WCAG verified
Typography Scale15 levels (display ‚Üí label) + font family + weights
Spacing System4px base unit (space-0 ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á space-20)
ShapeCorner radius tokens (none ‚Üí full)
ElevationShadow tokens (0-4 levels)

Component Hierarchy (Atomic Design)

  • Atoms: Button, Text Field, Checkbox, Radio, Toggle, Badge, Chip, Avatar
  • Molecules: Search Bar, List Item, Form Field, Menu Item, Tab
  • Organisms: App Bar, Navigation, Card, Dialog, Bottom Sheet, Data Table

Per-Component Spec

‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î: Anatomy, Variants, Sizes (S/M/L), States (6 states), Accessibility, Spacing Rules

Layout Adaptation Strategies

StrategyExample
ReflowCards stack vertical ‚Üí horizontal
RevealShow sidebar ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile

Nielsen's 10 Usability Heuristics

1. Visibility of System Status

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô feedback ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö loading states, progress indicators, status badges, toast notifications Spec checklist:

  • ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å action ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤ > 1 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ loading indicator
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ loading pattern: skeleton, spinner, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ progress bar
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ success/error feedback ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å form submission

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Ñ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô

‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏â‡∏∏‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏¥‡∏ô (emergency exit) ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‚Äî undo, redo, cancel, back

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö destructive actions, forms, wizards, modals Spec checklist:

‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ error message

6. Recognition Rather Than Recall

‡∏•‡∏î memory load ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å, actions, ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô

Laws of UX

Fitts's Law

‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á target ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢

Application in Spec:

  • Primary CTA: minimum 48x48dp (Android), 44x44pt (iOS)
  • ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ thumb zone (mobile) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ center of attention (web)
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ touch target size ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element

Hick's Law

‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° log ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å ‚Äî ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏á

Application in Spec:

  • Navigation items: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 5-7 items
  • Action buttons ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠: 1 primary, 1-2 secondary
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ categorization ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß

Jakob's Law

‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö/‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ

Application in Spec:

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ standard patterns (hamburger menu, tab bar, pull-to-refresh)
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ platform conventions ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°
  • ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å conventions

Miller's Law

‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì 7¬±2 ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô short-term memory

  • Chunk ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£ 0XX-XXX-XXXX)
  • Section headers ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å 5-7 items ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ grouping strategy ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö complex forms

Doherty Threshold

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô 400ms ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤ engagement

Application in Spec:

  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ perceived performance strategy (skeleton screens, optimistic UI)
  • Animations ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 300ms ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö micro-interactions
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ transition timing ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö page/screen changes

Von Restorff Effect (Isolation Effect)

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ô primary action

Application in Spec:

  • Primary CTA ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å secondary actions
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ visual hierarchy ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ color, size, position ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á emphasis

Postel's Law (Robustness Principle)

‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö input ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà output ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏°‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏î

Application in Spec:

  • ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö input ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ/‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ -)
  • ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ input parsing/formatting rules

Peak-End Rule

‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å peak moment ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ending ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏à‡∏ö‡∏î‡∏µ

Application in Spec:

  • ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö success state ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≥ (celebration animation, confetti)
  • Completion screen ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ next step ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ CTA ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô

Gestalt Principles

Proximity

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß

Spec: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ spacing ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á groups ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ spacing ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô group (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 24px ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á sections, 8px ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á items ‡πÉ‡∏ô section)

Similarity

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß

Spec: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ consistent styling ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö components ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° primary ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)

Continuity

‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏¥‡∏®‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á

Spec: ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î elements ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (alignment) ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ grid system

Closure

‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡∏£‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏π‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

Spec: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ card patterns, containers ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô

Common Region

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°

Spec: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ background color, cards, dividers ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ container styles ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô

How to Apply in Spec

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô Design Spec ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô "UX Principles Applied" ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö:

|----------|-----------|-----------|
| Primary CTA ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á form | Fitts's Law | ‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ thumb zone, ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á |

| ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î nav items ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠ 5 | Hick's Law + Miller's Law | ‡∏•‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à |
| Skeleton screen ‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î | Visibility of Status (H1) | ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô |
| ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ standard tab bar | Jakob's Law + Consistency (H4) | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö mental model ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ |

‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á "Principle" ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠:

Apple Human Interface Guidelines (HIG) Reference

‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Apple Human Interface Guidelines ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS, iPadOS, macOS

Design Principles

Apple HIG ‡∏¢‡∏∂‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç 6 ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠:

  1. Aesthetic Integrity ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô
  2. Consistency ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ system-provided components ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ patterns
  3. Direct Manipulation ‚Äî interact ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö content ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (gestures)
  4. Feedback ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å action ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ visual/haptic feedback
  5. Metaphors ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
  6. User Control ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏° ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á

Dynamic Type Support

  • ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å text style ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Dynamic Type (scalable)

Layout & Spacing

Safe Areas & Margins

Device Leading Margin Content Width
iPhone SE 16pt 343pt
iPhone 15 16pt 361pt
iPhone 15 Pro Max 16pt 398pt
iPad Mini 20pt ‚Äî
iPad Pro 11" 20pt ‚Äî
iPad Pro 12.9" 20pt ‚Äî

Standard Spacing

Value Usage
4pt Minimal (between related icons)
8pt Tight (related elements)
12pt Compact (list item internal)
16pt Standard (content margins, section gaps)
20pt Comfortable (iPad margins)
24pt Spacious (between major sections)
32pt Section breaks

Layout Grid

  • Base unit: 8pt
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á iOS layout behavior
  • ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏´‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á list items: 44pt (minimum tap height)

Key Components

Navigation Bar (UINavigationBar)

  • Height: 44pt (compact), 96pt (large title)
  • Large Title: 34pt, Bold, left-aligned
  • Back button: chevron + previous title
  • Bar buttons: SF Symbols (28pt), max 2 trailing

Tab Bar (UITabBar)

  • Height: 49pt (iPhone), 50pt (iPad)
  • Items: 2-5
  • Icon: 25pt x 25pt (SF Symbols)
  • Label: Caption 2 (10pt)
  • Active: tint color, Inactive: systemGray

Buttons

Type Height Corner Usage
Bordered Prominent 50pt 12pt Primary CTA
Bordered 50pt 12pt Secondary
Plain 44pt tap target None Tertiary, text-style
Destructive 50pt 12pt Delete, remove (red)

Lists / Tables

Style Usage
Inset Grouped Default for settings, forms (rounded corners, inset from edges)
Grouped Classic grouped (full width per section)
Plain Simple list, continuous (contacts, messages)
  • Row height: 44pt minimum
  • Cell padding: 16pt leading, 16pt trailing
  • Disclosure indicator: chevron.right (for drill-down navigation)
  • Swipe actions: leading (positive), trailing (destructive)

Sheets

Type Usage
Sheet (.sheet) Non-blocking, drag to dismiss
Full-screen cover Blocking, needs explicit dismiss
Popover iPad only, arrow points to source
  • Sheet corner radius: 10pt
  • Grabber: 36pt x 5pt, centered

Alerts

  • Title: Headline (17pt, Semibold)
  • Message: Footnote (13pt, Regular)
  • Buttons: 1-2 preferred, max 3
  • Destructive button: Red, on the left
  • Default/Cancel: Bold

Text Fields

  • Height: 36pt
  • Corner radius: 10pt
  • Background: tertiarySystemFill
  • Placeholder: tertiaryLabel color
  • Clear button on trailing edge when editing

Search Bar

  • Height: 36pt
  • Corner radius: 10pt
  • Magnifying glass icon on leading
  • Cancel button appears on focus

Navigation Patterns

iPhone

  1. Tab Bar + Navigation Stack ‚Äî most common
    • Tab bar: top-level destinations (3-5)
    • Navigation stack: drill-down within each tab
  2. Modal Sheets ‚Äî for focused tasks
    • Present modally for creation/editing flows
    • Swipe down to dismiss (non-blocking)

iPad

  1. Split View ‚Äî master-detail
    • Sidebar: 320pt width
    • Content: fills remaining
  2. Tab Bar (compact) ‚Äî Sidebar (regular)
    • Adaptive navigation

Transitions

Type Usage Direction
Push Navigate deeper Left to right (LTR)
Pop Navigate back Right to left
Modal present Show sheet/fullscreen Bottom to top
Modal dismiss Close sheet Top to bottom / swipe down

Motion & Animation

Duration Guidelines

Type Duration Usage
Quick feedback 100ms Toggle, selection
Standard 250ms Sheet present, nav push
Complex 350-500ms Full-screen transitions

Spring Animation (preferred)

  • iOS prefers spring-based animation over easing curves
  • Default spring: response: 0.3, dampingFraction: 0.8
  • Bouncy: response: 0.4, dampingFraction: 0.6

Haptic Feedback

Type Usage
Impact (light) Button tap, toggle
Impact (medium) Snap to position
Impact (heavy) Significant action complete
Notification (success) Task complete
Notification (warning) Caution action
Notification (error) Error occurred
Selection Scrolling through picker

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ haptic feedback ‡πÉ‡∏ô spec ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS apps

Accessibility

Minimum Sizes

  • Touch target: 44pt x 44pt minimum
  • Spacing between targets: >= 8pt
  • Text: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ Dynamic Type support

VoiceOver

  • ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ accessibility label
  • Images: accessibilityLabel ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö meaningful images
  • Decorative images: isAccessibilityElement = false
  • Group related elements ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ accessibilityElement container

Color Contrast

  • Text: 4.5:1 minimum (AA)
  • Large text (>= 18pt): 3:1
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ system colors ‡∏ã‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö accessibility ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  • Support Increase Contrast mode

Reduce Motion

  • ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Reduce Motion preference
  • ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà animation ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ cross-dissolve ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Reduce Motion ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

Platform Differences

iOS vs Android ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Spec

Feature iOS (HIG) Android (Material)
Primary nav Tab Bar (bottom) Bottom Nav / Nav Rail
Back Swipe from left edge System back button/gesture
Action placement Top-right in nav bar FAB or top app bar
Destructive Leading swipe (red) Trailing swipe or dialog
Sheet Drag handle, swipe dismiss Bottom sheet with handle
Font SF Pro (system) Roboto (system)
Units pt (points) dp (density-independent pixels)
Min touch 44pt x 44pt 48dp x 48dp
Alert buttons Stacked or side-by-side Always side-by-side

Design Tokens

Spacing (Base unit: 4dp)

Token Value Usage
spacing-xs 4dp Icon padding
spacing-sm 8dp Tight element spacing
spacing-md 16dp Default content padding
spacing-lg 24dp Section spacing
spacing-xl 32dp Large section spacing
spacing-2xl 48dp Page margins (compact)

Key Components

Buttons

Type Height Min Width Corner Usage
Filled 40dp 48dp 20dp (full) Primary CTA
Outlined 40dp 48dp 20dp Secondary actions
Text 40dp 48dp 20dp Low-emphasis
Elevated 40dp 48dp 20dp Medium emphasis with shadow
Tonal 40dp 48dp 20dp Medium emphasis, no shadow
FAB 56dp 56dp 16dp Primary floating action
Extended FAB 56dp - 16dp FAB with label

Text Fields

Type Height Usage
Filled 56dp Default, high density forms
Outlined 56dp Lower density, clearer boundaries

States: Rest, Focused, Error, Disabled

  • Label floats on focus
  • Helper text below (12sp, Body Small)
  • Error text replaces helper in error state (Error color)

Cards

Type Elevation Border Usage
Elevated Level 1 None Default
Filled Level 0 None Secondary surface color
Outlined Level 0 1dp outline Clear boundaries

Padding: 16dp all sides (minimum) Corner radius: 12dp (Medium)

Dialogs

  • Width: 280-560dp
  • Corner radius: 28dp (Extra Large)
  • Elevation: Level 5
  • Title: Headline Small (24sp)
  • Body: Body Medium (14sp)
  • Actions: Text buttons, right-aligned

Bottom Sheets

  • Corner radius: 28dp (top corners only)
  • Handle: 32dp x 4dp, centered, 22dp from top
  • Standard: pushes content up
  • Modal: overlay with scrim

Navigation Bar (Bottom)

  • Height: 80dp
  • Items: 3-5
  • Icon: 24dp
  • Label: Label Medium (12sp)
  • Active indicator: pill shape (64dp x 32dp)

Duration

Category Duration Usage

Easing

Type Curve Usage
Emphasized cubic-bezier(0.2, 0, 0, 1) Most transitions
Emphasized Decelerate cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0, 1) Enter/appear

Accessibility

Touch Targets

  • Minimum: 48dp x 48dp
  • Recommended: 56dp x 56dp ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö primary actions
  • Spacing between targets: >= 8dp

Color Contrast (WCAG 2.1)

  • Normal text: 4.5:1 minimum (AA)
  • Large text (>= 18sp regular, >= 14sp bold): 3:1 minimum
  • Icons and UI components: 3:1 minimum

What Are Design Tokens

Design Tokens ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design decisions ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡πà‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á design (Figma) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ code ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏™‡∏µ, font size, spacing, border-radius

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ custom design system ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î tokens ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô spec

Token Naming Convention

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö: semantic/{category}/{property}/{variant}

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á:

semantic/gray-neutral/fg/high            ‚Üí #1B1D22
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/mid-on-white    ‚Üí #6A6E83
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/white           ‚Üí #FFFFFF
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/lightgray       ‚Üí #F8F8F9

semantic/primary/fg/high                 ‚Üí #EC599D
semantic/primary/bg/mid                  ‚Üí #EC599D
semantic/primary/border/high             ‚Üí #EC599D

semantic/secondary/fg/high               ‚Üí #7279FB
semantic/error/fg/high                   ‚Üí #EA244F
semantic/success/bg/high                 ‚Üí #559652
semantic/info/border/low                 ‚Üí #CDEDF9

semantic/alpha-black/bg/mid              ‚Üí #101114 @ 70%
semantic/alpha-white/fg/low              ‚Üí #FFFFFF @ 50%

semantic/support/red/fg/low              ‚Üí #EA244F
semantic/support/violet/bg/mid           ‚Üí #AAAFFD

spacing-xs                               ‚Üí 4px
spacing-sm                               ‚Üí 8px
spacing-md                               ‚Üí 16px
spacing-lg                               ‚Üí 24px

font-size-body-md                        ‚Üí 14px
font-weight-heading                      ‚Üí 700
font-family-primary                      ‚Üí "Inter"

radius-sm                                ‚Üí 4px
radius-md                                ‚Üí 8px
radius-lg                                ‚Üí 16px
radius-full                              ‚Üí 9999px

shadow-sm                                ‚Üí 0 1px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)
shadow-md                                ‚Üí 0 4px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.12)

z-index-dropdown                         ‚Üí 100
z-index-modal                            ‚Üí 200
z-index-toast                            ‚Üí 300

Token Categories

1. Color Tokens (Semantic System)

Source: Figma Tokens export (Mode 1). Token paths use semantic/{category}/{property}/{variant} format. For alpha colors, value is shown as hex @ opacity%.

1.1 Gray-Neutral

Token Hex Alpha Description
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/white #FFFFFF 100% White foreground
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/low-on-white #9A9DAD 100% Low-contrast text on white
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/mid-on-white #6A6E83 100% Medium-contrast text on white
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/mid-on-gray #3F414E 100% Medium-contrast text on gray
semantic/gray-neutral/fg/high #1B1D22 100% High-contrast foreground (near-black)
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/white #FFFFFF 100% White background
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/lightgray #F8F8F9 100% Light gray background
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/midgray #EBECEF 100% Medium gray background
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/darkgray #CFD1D9 100% Dark gray background
semantic/gray-neutral/bg/black #1B1D22 100% Black background
semantic/gray-neutral/border/white #FFFFFF 100% White border
semantic/gray-neutral/border/lightgray #F8F8F9 100% Light gray border
semantic/gray-neutral/border/midgray #EBECEF 100% Medium gray border
semantic/gray-neutral/border/darkgray #CFD1D9 100% Dark gray border

## Design Tokens

| semantic/error/fg/high | #EA244F | Error states |
| ... | ... | ... |

| ... | ... | ... |

Figma Integration Notes

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Designer ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥ Tokens ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

  1. Figma Variables: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Color, Number, String variables ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° token ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î

    • ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Collections: Colors, Typography, Spacing, etc.
    • ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á modes: Light / Dark ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö color tokens

  2. Figma Styles: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Text Styles, Color Styles, Effect Styles

    • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° token naming convention

  3. Component Properties: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Figma component properties ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á variants

    • State: default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled
    • Size: small, medium, large
    • Type: primary, secondary, tertiary

  4. Auto Layout: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ spacing tokens ‡πÉ‡∏ô auto layout settings

    • Item spacing = spacing token
    • Padding = spacing token

  5. Plugins ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢:

    • Tokens Studio for Figma: ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ design tokens
    • Figma Variables: native Figma feature (preferred)

FontAwesome Icons Reference for Figma MCP

‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å MCP ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á vector icon ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ text placeholder ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß dev ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô FontAwesome component ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô implement ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Icon ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma MCP

Pattern: Icon Placeholder

create_text({
  text: "‚¨ú",           // placeholder character
  name: "icon/fa-home", // ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ layer ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô FA icon name
  fontSize: 20,
  fontColor: {r, g, b},
  parentId: "container-id"
})

‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏á Naming Convention

  • Layer name: icon/fa-{icon-name}
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á: icon/fa-calendar, icon/fa-user, icon/fa-bell
  • Dev ‡∏à‡∏∞ map ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ layer ‚Üí <FontAwesomeIcon icon="fa-{name}" />

Install FontAwesome (for Dev)

  • ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Figma ‚Üí ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ô Plugin "Talk to Figma" ‚Üí copy channel ID
  • ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ connect ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°: "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Talk to Figma Plugin ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å channel ID ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö"

2. Document & Selection

Command Parameters Description
get_document_info ‚Äî ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• document ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (pages, frames)

read_my_design ‚Äî ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á selection (all node details)

scan_text_nodes nodeId ‡∏´‡∏≤ text nodes ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô node ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏

3. Creation Tools

Frames & Containers

create_frame({
  x, y, width, height,        // required
  name?,                       // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ layer
  parentId?,                   // ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ parent ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢ (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á insert_child ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å)
  fillColor?: {r, g, b, a?},  // ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô (0-1)
  strokeColor?: {r, g, b, a?}, strokeWeight?,
  // Auto Layout (‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢)
  layoutMode?: "NONE" | "HORIZONTAL" | "VERTICAL",
  layoutSizingHorizontal?: "FIXED" | "HUG" | "FILL",
  layoutSizingVertical?: "FIXED" | "HUG" | "FILL",
  primaryAxisAlignItems?: "MIN" | "MAX" | "CENTER" | "SPACE_BETWEEN",
  counterAxisAlignItems?: "MIN" | "MAX" | "CENTER" | "BASELINE",
  itemSpacing?,
  paddingTop?, paddingRight?, paddingBottom?, paddingLeft?,
  layoutWrap?: "NO_WRAP" | "WRAP"
})

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç: create_frame ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á auto layout + ‡∏™‡∏µ + parentId ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á

Command Parameters Description

‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ rectangle ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ellipse, polygon, star

5. Auto Layout Tools

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç: ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á set_auto_layout ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô 5 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á:

Command Parameters Description
set_layout_mode nodeId, layoutMode, layoutWrap? ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á layout direction: NONE/HORIZONTAL/VERTICAL
set_padding nodeId, paddingTop?, paddingRight?, paddingBottom?, paddingLeft? ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á padding
set_axis_align nodeId, primaryAxisAlignItems?, counterAxisAlignItems? ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á alignment
set_layout_sizing nodeId, layoutSizingHorizontal?, layoutSizingVertical? ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á sizing mode: FIXED/HUG/FILL
set_item_spacing nodeId, itemSpacing?, counterAxisSpacing? ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á spacing ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á children

‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏•‡∏±‡∏î: ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Auto Layout ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Frame

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ create_frame ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° params ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢:

create_frame({
  name: "Card",
  x: 0, y: 0, width: 361, height: 200,
  layoutMode: "VERTICAL",
  itemSpacing: 12,
  paddingTop: 16, paddingRight: 16, paddingBottom: 16, paddingLeft: 16,
  primaryAxisAlignItems: "MIN",
  counterAxisAlignItems: "MIN",
  layoutSizingHorizontal: "FIXED",
  layoutSizingVertical: "HUG",
  fillColor: {r: 1, g: 1, b: 1}
})

Alignment Values Reference

Value primaryAxisAlignItems counterAxisAlignItems
MIN ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ (H) / ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô (V) ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô (H) / ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ (V)
CENTER ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á
MAX ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤ (H) / ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (V) ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á (H) / ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤ (V)
SPACE_BETWEEN ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (ignores itemSpacing) ‚Äî
BASELINE ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ counter axis, ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î baseline text

6. Text Tools

Command Parameters Description
set_text_content nodeId, text ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô text content
set_multiple_text_contents nodeId (parent), text[] ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô text ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

set_multiple_text_contents format

set_multiple_text_contents({
  nodeId: "parent-id",
  text: [
    { nodeId: "text-1-id", text: "New text 1" },
    { nodeId: "text-2-id", text: "New text 2" }
  ]
})

‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ: set_font_name, set_font_size, set_font_weight, set_letter_spacing, set_line_height, set_text_case, set_text_decoration, load_font_async ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ font ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô create_text ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô (fontSize, fontWeight, fontColor) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á

7. Component Tools

Command Parameters Description
get_local_components ‚Äî ‡∏î‡∏π components ‡πÉ‡∏ô file
create_component_instance componentKey, x, y ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á instance ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å component
get_instance_overrides nodeId? ‡∏î‡∏π overrides ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á instance (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ nodeId ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ selection)
set_instance_overrides sourceInstanceId, targetNodeIds[] Copy overrides ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å source ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á targets

‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ: get_remote_components ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ local components

Command Parameters Description

9. Connector Tools

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏° (flow diagrams, prototyping visualization)

11. Screenshot & Design Context (Figma Remote MCP)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ server figma (remote) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ fileKey ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ nodeId ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å URL

‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å fileKey ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ nodeId ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å URL

URL: https://figma.com/design/ABC123/MyFile?node-id=1-2
‚Üí fileKey = "ABC123"
‚Üí nodeId = "1:2"  (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô - ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô :)
Command Parameters Description
get_screenshot fileKey, nodeId ‡∏ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á node
get_design_context fileKey, nodeId ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design + generate UI code
get_metadata fileKey, nodeId ‡∏î‡∏π structure ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö XML (node IDs, types, positions)
get_variable_defs fileKey, nodeId ‡∏î‡∏π design variables ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô node
whoami ‚Äî ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà login ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

Use Cases

  • get_screenshot: ‡∏î‡∏π preview ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ reference design
  • get_design_context: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ generate code ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à design
  • get_metadata: ‡∏î‡∏π structure ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á file ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤ node IDs

14. Import HTML to Figma (html-to-design MCP)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ server html-to-design (remote) ‚Äî ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layers ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Claude

Prerequisites

  1. ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á plugin html.to.design (by divRIOTS) ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
  2. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î plugin ‚Üí tab MCP ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î toggle "Enable MCP endpoint"
  3. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ STATUS: connected (‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß) ‡πÉ‡∏ô plugin

Available Tools

Command Parameters Description
import_html html, css?, js?, name? ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML code ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layers
import_url url, name? ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á URL ‡πÑ‡∏õ import ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layers

import_html ‚Äî ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML Code

import_html({
  html: "<div class='card'>...</div>",
  css: ".card { display: flex; ... }",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
  • ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML + CSS ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á ‚Üí plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layers ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á serve file ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô URL
  • ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á manual copy/paste ‡πÉ‡∏ô plugin
  • Class names ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names

import_url ‚Äî ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á URL

import_url({
  url: "http://localhost:3000/login-preview.html",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
  • ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö ‚Üí plugin import ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
  • ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á serve file ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô (Live Server, npx serve .)
  • ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô (multi-page, external assets)

Workflow: Claude ‚Üí HTML ‚Üí Figma

1. Claude ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview (Step 3 ‡πÉ‡∏ô UI Design Spec)
2. User review ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser + iterate ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à
3. Claude ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô import_html ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ import_url
4. Plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á HTML ‚Üí Figma layers ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
5. User fine-tune ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (font, sizing, components)

Tips

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ import_html ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ HTML ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å (single component, single screen)
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ import_url ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ HTML ‡∏°‡∏µ external assets (fonts, images) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤
  • ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å "send to Figma" ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ "send to html.to.design" ‡πÉ‡∏ô prompt ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ trigger import
  • ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ plugin ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î MCP endpoint ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import

15. Common Patterns

Pattern 1: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Mobile Screen (iPhone 15 Pro)

// ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á main frame ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° auto layout + ‡∏™‡∏µ ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
create_frame({
  name: "Login Screen",
  x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 852,
  fillColor: {r: 1, g: 1, b: 1},
  layoutMode: "VERTICAL",
  paddingTop: 0, paddingRight: 16, paddingBottom: 0, paddingLeft: 16,
  primaryAxisAlignItems: "MIN",
  counterAxisAlignItems: "MIN",
  layoutSizingHorizontal: "FIXED",
  layoutSizingVertical: "FIXED",
  itemSpacing: 0
})
set_corner_radius(nodeId, 47)

Pattern 2: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Text Field

// 1. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á container ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° auto layout + parentId
create_frame({
  name: "Email Field",
  parentId: "screen-id",          // ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ parent ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
  x: 0, y: 0, width: 361, height: 50,
  fillColor: {r: 0.46, g: 0.46, b: 0.5, a: 0.12},
  layoutMode: "HORIZONTAL",
  itemSpacing: 10,
  paddingLeft: 12, paddingRight: 12, paddingTop: 0, paddingBottom: 0,
  counterAxisAlignItems: "CENTER"
})
set_corner_radius(container_id, 10)

// 2. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á text ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ container ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
create_text({
  text: "Email address",
  x: 0, y: 0,
  fontSize: 17,
  fontColor: {r: 0.24, g: 0.24, b: 0.26, a: 0.6},
  parentId: "container-id"       // ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ container
})

Pattern 3: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Button

create_frame({
  name: "Log In Button",
  parentId: "screen-id",
  x: 0, y: 0, width: 361, height: 50,
  fillColor: {r: 0, g: 0.48, b: 1},
  layoutMode: "HORIZONTAL",
  primaryAxisAlignItems: "CENTER",
  counterAxisAlignItems: "CENTER"
})
set_corner_radius(button_id, 12)

create_text({
  text: "Log In",
  x: 0, y: 0,
  fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700,
  fontColor: {r: 1, g: 1, b: 1},
  parentId: "button-id"
})

Pattern 4: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Card

create_frame({
  name: "Notification Card",
  parentId: "screen-id",
  x: 0, y: 0, width: 361, height: 120,
  fillColor: {r: 1, g: 1, b: 1},
  strokeColor: {r: 0.89, g: 0.89, b: 0.91},
  strokeWeight: 1,
  layoutMode: "VERTICAL",
  itemSpacing: 8,
  paddingTop: 16, paddingRight: 16, paddingBottom: 16, paddingLeft: 16,
  layoutSizingVertical: "HUG"
})
set_corner_radius(card_id, 12)

Pattern 5: Batch Text Update

// ‡∏´‡∏≤ text nodes ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
scan_text_nodes(parentNodeId)

// ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß
set_multiple_text_contents({
  nodeId: "parent-id",
  text: [
    { nodeId: "title-id", text: "New Title" },
    { nodeId: "subtitle-id", text: "New Subtitle" },
    { nodeId: "body-id", text: "New body text here" }
  ]
})

Pattern 6: Clone & Modify (‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Variants)

// Clone element
clone_node(nodeId: "original-card", x: 420, y: 0)

// ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç clone
set_fill_color(clone_id, r: 0.95, g: 0.95, b: 0.97)
scan_text_nodes(clone_id)
set_text_content(text_id, "Variant B")

Pattern 7: Read Existing Design

// ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
get_document_info()

// ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å
read_my_design()

// ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma Remote (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ fileKey + nodeId)
get_screenshot(fileKey, nodeId)
get_design_context(fileKey, nodeId)

16. Color Conversion

Figma MCP ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏µ RGBA ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö 0-1 (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ 0-255)

Hex to Figma RGBA Formula

r = parseInt(hex.slice(1,3), 16) / 255
g = parseInt(hex.slice(3,5), 16) / 255
b = parseInt(hex.slice(5,7), 16) / 255

Common Colors

Color Hex Figma RGBA
systemBlue (light) #007AFF r=0, g=0.478, b=1
systemRed (light) #FF3B30 r=1, g=0.231, b=0.188
systemGreen (light) #34C759 r=0.204, g=0.78, b=0.349
Black #000000 r=0, g=0, b=0
White #FFFFFF r=1, g=1, b=1
M3 Primary #6750A4 r=0.404, g=0.314, b=0.643
M3 Surface #FFFBFE r=1, g=0.984, b=0.996
Gray 100 #F5F5F5 r=0.961, g=0.961, b=0.961
Gray 300 #E0E0E0 r=0.878, g=0.878, b=0.878
Gray 600 #757575 r=0.459, g=0.459, b=0.459
Gray 900 #212121 r=0.129, g=0.129, b=0.129

17. Smart Frame Positioning (‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô Frame ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç: ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á frame ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á frame ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠

Pattern: Scan Before Create

// ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 1: ‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô document ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π frame ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
get_document_info()

// ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 2: ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î position/size ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á frame ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô page
get_nodes_info(nodeIds: ["frame-1-id", "frame-2-id", ...])

// ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà 3: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö
// - ‡∏´‡∏≤ maxX = max(frame.x + frame.width) ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å frame
// - ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á frame ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà x = maxX + GAP

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á

GAP = 100  // ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏´‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á frames (px)

// ‡∏´‡∏≤ bounding box ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å frame ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà
existingFrames = get_document_info().children.filter(type == "FRAME" | "SECTION")
nodesInfo = get_nodes_info(existingFrames.map(id))

// ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ (‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤)
maxX = 0
for each frame in nodesInfo:
  rightEdge = frame.x + frame.width
  if rightEdge > maxX:
    maxX = rightEdge

newFrameX = maxX + GAP
newFrameY = 0  // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà y=0 ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ align ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö frame ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å)

‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

// 1. ‡∏™‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
docInfo = get_document_info()
// ‚Üí ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠ Frame A ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà x=0, w=393 / Frame B ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà x=493, w=393

// 2. ‡∏î‡∏π details
nodesInfo = get_nodes_info(["frame-a-id", "frame-b-id"])
// ‚Üí Frame A: x=0, y=0, w=393, h=852
// ‚Üí Frame B: x=493, y=0, w=393, h=852

// 3. ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì
// maxX = 493 + 393 = 886
// newX = 886 + 100 = 986

// 4. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á frame ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö
create_frame({ x: 986, y: 0, width: 393, height: 852, ... })

Layout Strategies

Strategy ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì
‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤ Default - ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô x = maxX + GAP
‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á y = maxY + GAP
Grid ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ frame (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô responsive) ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å 3 frame ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ñ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

Grid Layout ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Responsive Design

COLS = 3          // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô columns
GAP = 100         // ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡∏´‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
FRAME_WIDTH = 393 // ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á frame

for i in range(totalFrames):
  col = i % COLS
  row = i // COLS  (integer division)
  x = startX + col * (FRAME_WIDTH + GAP)
  y = startY + row * (FRAME_HEIGHT + GAP)

18. Icon Placeholder Pattern (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ FontAwesome)

‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å MCP ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á vector icon ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ text placeholder ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ

// ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Unicode placeholder + ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ layer ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô FA icon name
create_text({
  text: "üìÖ",              // placeholder emoji/symbol
  name: "icon/fa-calendar", // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ layer = FA icon name
  fontSize: 20,
  fontColor: {r: 0.42, g: 0.447, b: 0.502},
  parentId: "container-id"
})

Naming Convention

  • Format: icon/fa-{icon-name}
  • Dev ‡∏à‡∏∞ map ‚Üí <FontAwesomeIcon icon="fa-{name}" />
  • ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î icon ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà references/fontawesome-icons.md

19. Exact Color Conversion (Hex ‚Üí Figma RGBA)

‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏®‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏° ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ 3 ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠ 2 ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á

21. Post-Creation Verification Pattern

‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á verify ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö spec

Pattern: Verify Main Frame

// ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á main screen frame
frameInfo = get_node_info(mainFrameId)

// ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à dimensions
if frameInfo.width != expectedWidth || frameInfo.height != expectedHeight:
  resize_node(mainFrameId, expectedWidth, expectedHeight)

// ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à fill color (‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ RGBA)
if frameInfo.fills[0].color != expectedColor:
  set_fill_color(mainFrameId, r, g, b)

Pattern: Verify Children

// ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á children ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
childIds = [child1Id, child2Id, ...]
childrenInfo = get_nodes_info(childIds)

for each child in childrenInfo:
  // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à size
  if |child.width - expectedWidth| > 2:
    resize_node(child.id, expectedWidth, expectedHeight)

  // ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à color
  if child.fills && child.fills[0].color != expectedColor:
    set_fill_color(child.id, r, g, b)

Tolerance

  • Dimensions: ¬±1px (auto-layout ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏© sub-pixel)
  • Colors: ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ RGBA ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ exact conversion ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Section 18)
  • Spacing: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à itemSpacing ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô parent frame info

When to Verify

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏∞ ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£
‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á main frame get_node_info() ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à w, h, fill
‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á children ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î get_nodes_info() ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à w, h ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ child
‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á auto-layout get_node_info() ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ frame ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà resize ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î
‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ get_node_info(mainFrame) ‚Üí snapshot ‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢

22. Font Handling (‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠)

MCP ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô create_text

Parameter ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
fontSize ‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á fontSize: 17
fontWeight ‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á fontWeight: 700 (‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö 400, 700)
fontColor ‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á fontColor: {r: 0, g: 0, b: 0}
fontFamily ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ Figma ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ default font (‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Inter)
lineHeight ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
letterSpacing ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
textDecoration ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
textCase ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á

Parameter ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ
text content ‚úÖ set_text_content(nodeId, text)
fill color (text bg) ‚úÖ set_fill_color(nodeId, r, g, b)
fontSize ‚ùå ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
fontWeight ‚ùå ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

CSS fontWeight ‚Üí Figma Mapping

MCP ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ 400 (Regular) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ 700 (Bold):

CSS font-weight ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ Figma fontWeight ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏
100 (Thin) 100 400 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Regular
200 (ExtraLight) 200 400 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Regular
300 (Light) 300 400 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Regular
normal / 400 (Regular) 400 400 ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
500 (Medium) 500 400 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Regular (‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤)
600 (SemiBold) 600 700 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Bold
bold / 700 (Bold) 700 700 ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
800 (ExtraBold) 800 700 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Bold
900 (Black) 900 700 ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Bold

‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á text ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à

‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:

"Text ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ fontSize ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ fontWeight ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà font family ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö preview (Figma ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ default font) ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô font family:

  1. ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å text ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (Cmd+A ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô frame)
  2. ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô font ‡πÉ‡∏ô Properties panel ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤
  3. ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ SF Pro
  4. ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Android ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Roboto
  5. ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Custom ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ font ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° brand guidelines"

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ô MCP (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á)

  • ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Ellipse, Polygon, Star
  • ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á/‡∏•‡∏ö/‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Page
  • Group/Ungroup nodes
  • ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô font family/style ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á text ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á effects (shadow, blur)
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á text decoration (underline, strikethrough)
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á line height, letter spacing, paragraph spacing
  • Rename node
  • Get remote components (team library)

23. HTML to Figma ‚Äî Best Practices

‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô html-to-design MCP (‡∏î‡∏π Section 14) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ manual import ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô plugin

Plugin: html.to.design (by divRIOTS)

  • MCP (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥): ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏° html-to-design MCP ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ import_html / import_url ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Claude (‡∏î‡∏π Section 14)
  • Manual: Figma ‚Üí Plugins ‚Üí html.to.design ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á HTML page ‚Üí Import
  • ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ manual ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î HTML ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô URL (Live Server ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ npx serve .)

HTML Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Import

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô HTML/CSS ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏é‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

CSS ‚Üí Figma Mapping

HTML/CSS Figma Result ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏
display: flex Auto Layout ‚Äî
flex-direction: column Vertical Auto Layout ‚Äî
flex-direction: row Horizontal Auto Layout ‚Äî
gap: 16px Item Spacing = 16 ‚Äî
padding: 16px Padding = 16 (all sides) ‚Äî
padding: 12px 16px paddingTop/Bottom = 12, Left/Right = 16 ‚Äî
border-radius: 12px Corner Radius = 12 ‚Äî
width: 100% (flex child) layoutSizingHorizontal = FILL ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ child ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á flex
width: 200px Fixed Width = 200 ‚Äî
background-color: #EC599D Fill Color ‚Äî
color: #1B1D22 Text Color ‚Äî
font-size: 16px Font Size = 16 ‚Äî
font-weight: 700 Font Weight = Bold ‚Äî
box-shadow Effect > Drop Shadow ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á plugin ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö

Class Names ‚Üí Layer Names

Plugin ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ class name ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô layer name ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:

<!-- ‚úÖ ‡∏î‡∏µ ‚Äî layer name ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ -->
<div class="login-form">
  <input class="email-field" />
  <button class="login-button">‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö</button>
</div>

<!-- ‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ ‚Äî layer name ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ -->

  <input class="w-full" />
  <button class="bg-pink-500">‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö</button>
</div>

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥

  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox/grid (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute position) ‚Üí Auto Layout
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS Variables ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö colors ‚Üí ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö
  • ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á class names ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Üí Figma layer names ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ semantic HTML (<header>, <main>, <section>) ‚Üí clean hierarchy
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Google Fonts ‚Üí font ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å map (‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma)
  • ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ inline SVG ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö icons ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô vector ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á

  • absolute/fixed position ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ Auto Layout
  • Tailwind/Bootstrap class names ‚Üí layer names ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢
  • Complex CSS animations ‚Üí ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
  • External images via URL ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ inline SVG ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ base64 ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô
  • Nested flex ‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ ‚Üí Figma layer hierarchy ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô

‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á Import ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

  1. Font: ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô font ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ (LINE Seed Sans TH, SF Pro, Roboto)
  2. Sizing mode: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à FILL/HUG/FIXED ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
  3. Layer names: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö rename ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  4. Components: ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á repeated elements ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma components
  5. Styles: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á color styles / text styles ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å imported values

# Figma UI Design Specification Skill

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ UI Design Specification ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° preview ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read Design Principles ‚Üí 3. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 4. Iterate (Browser) ‚Üí 5. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)
```

‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á 5 ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ flow ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á skill:

1. **Requirements**: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Jira card ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô jira-req-analysis skill)
2. **Design Principles**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô references ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
3. **Preview**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Static HTML file (.html) ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma
4. **Iterate**: User ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î HTML ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser + ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å Claude ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç ‚Üí refresh ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
5. **Import to Figma**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ html-to-design MCP ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (`import_html` / `import_url`)

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

Requirements ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å:
- **User ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á
- **Jira card analysis** ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ user ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `jira-req-analysis` skill ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ structured data (User Stories, Screen List, State Matrix, Components, User Flow) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏õ Step 2 ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢
- **Figma reference design** ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ get_screenshot/get_design_context ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ structured requirements ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Platform**: Mobile (iOS/Android), Web, Desktop, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Cross-platform?
- **Screen/Component**: ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ component ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **User Goal**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ?
- **Detail Level**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Wireframe (Lo-fi) ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Hi-fi UI spec?
- **Design System**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Material Design, HIG, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ custom design system?
- **Constraints**: ‡∏°‡∏µ brand guidelines, ‡∏™‡∏µ, font ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Reference Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô reference ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ get_screenshot/get_design_context ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ)

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Principles

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform:

```
references/ux-principles.md        ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (Nielsen's + Laws of UX + Gestalt)
references/material-design.md      ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Android / Web (Material Design 3)
references/hig.md                  ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS / macOS (Apple HIG)
references/design-tokens.md        ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Custom Design System tokens
```

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/ux-principles.md` **‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á**

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö platform-specific:
- Android / Material ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° `references/material-design.md`
- iOS / Apple ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° `references/hig.md`
- Cross-platform ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ reference design URL:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_screenshot(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π visual
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_design_context(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design details
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `get_metadata(fileKey, nodeId)` ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π structure

---

## Step 3: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Interactive Preview (Static HTML)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html` self-contained ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma

### Preview ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:

1. **iPhone/Android frame** ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 393x852 ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iPhone 15 Pro) ‚Äî CSS-only
2. **Status bar** ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤, battery, signal) ‚Äî HTML+CSS
3. **‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° spec ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Design Tokens (CSS Variables)
4. **Light/Dark mode toggle** ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö theme ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)
5. **State switcher** ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô state: empty, filled, error, loading, success (vanilla JS)
6. **Interactive elements** ‚Äî ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å input, ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° ‡∏î‡∏π state ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á (vanilla JS)
7. **Spec info panel** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç (frame size, font, spacing, colors)

### HTML Template:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="th">
<head>
  <meta charset="UTF-8">
  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
  <title>[Screen Name] Preview</title>
  <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=LINE+Seed+Sans+TH:wght@400;700;800&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
  <style>
    :root {
      /* Design Tokens ‚Äî ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å semantic system (references/design-tokens.md) */
      --primary-fg-high: #EC599D;
      --primary-fg-low: #FDEFF5;
      --primary-bg-mid: #EC599D;
      --primary-bg-low: #FBD5E5;
      --primary-bg-lowest: #FDEFF5;
      --secondary-fg-high: #7279FB;
      --secondary-bg-mid: #7279FB;
      --secondary-bg-lowest: #EEEFFE;
      --gray-fg-high: #1B1D22;
      --gray-fg-mid-on-white: #6A6E83;
      --gray-fg-mid-on-gray: #3F414E;
      --gray-fg-low: #9A9DAD;
      --gray-fg-white: #FFFFFF;
      --gray-bg-white: #FFFFFF;
      --gray-bg-lightgray: #F8F8F9;
      --gray-bg-midgray: #EBECEF;
      --gray-bg-darkgray: #CFD1D9;
      --gray-bg-black: #1B1D22;
      --gray-border-midgray: #EBECEF;
      --gray-border-darkgray: #CFD1D9;
      --error-fg-high: #EA244F;
      --error-bg-lowest: #FDECF0;
      --warning-fg-high: #F8C135;
      --warning-bg-lowest: #FEF8E8;
      --success-fg-high: #559652;
      --success-bg-lowest: #EEF6EE;
      --info-fg-high: #0386B3;
      --info-bg-lowest: #E6F4F9;

      /* Typography ‚Äî LINE Seed Sans TH */
      --font-family: 'LINE Seed Sans TH', sans-serif;
      --heading-1: 800 48px/56px var(--font-family);
      --heading-2: 700 40px/48px var(--font-family);
      --heading-3: 700 32px/40px var(--font-family);
      --label-1: 700 20px/28px var(--font-family);
      --label-2: 700 18px/24px var(--font-family);
      --label-3: 700 16px/22px var(--font-family);
      --label-4: 700 14px/20px var(--font-family);
      --caption-1: 400 20px/28px var(--font-family);
      --caption-2: 400 18px/24px var(--font-family);
      --caption-3: 400 16px/22px var(--font-family);
      --caption-4: 400 14px/20px var(--font-family);

      /* Spacing */
      --space-xs: 4px;
      --space-sm: 8px;
      --space-md: 12px;
      --space-lg: 16px;
      --space-xl: 20px;
      --space-2xl: 24px;
      --space-3xl: 32px;

      /* Shape */
      --radius-sm: 8px;
      --radius-md: 12px;
      --radius-lg: 16px;
      --radius-full: 9999px;
    }

    * { margin: 0; padding: 0; box-sizing: border-box; }
    body { font-family: var(--font-family); background: #E5E5E5; display: flex; justify-content: center; padding: 20px; }

    /* ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox layout (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute positioning) */
    /* ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ semantic HTML: header, main, nav, section, footer */
    /* Class names ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ (‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names) */
  </style>
</head>
<body>
  <!-- Phone Frame -->
  <div class="phone-frame" style="width:393px; min-height:852px; background:var(--gray-bg-white); border-radius:40px; overflow:hidden; box-shadow:0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.12); display:flex; flex-direction:column;">
    <!-- Status Bar -->
    <div class="status-bar" style="display:flex; justify-content:space-between; align-items:center; padding:12px 24px; font:var(--caption-4); color:var(--gray-fg-high);">
      <span>9:41</span>
      <span><!-- signal + wifi + battery icons --></span>
    </div>

    <!-- Main Content -->
    <main style="flex:1; display:flex; flex-direction:column; padding:0 var(--space-lg);">
      <!-- Content here -->
    </main>
  </div>

  <!-- Control Panel (outside phone frame) -->
  <div class="control-panel" style="margin-left:24px; padding:16px; background:white; border-radius:12px; height:fit-content;">
    <button onclick="toggleTheme()">Light/Dark</button>
    <button onclick="setState('default')">Default</button>
    <button onclick="setState('filled')">Filled</button>
    <button onclick="setState('error')">Error</button>
    <button onclick="setState('loading')">Loading</button>
    <button onclick="setState('success')">Success</button>
    <button onclick="setState('empty')">Empty</button>
  </div>

  <script>
    // Vanilla JS ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö toggle, state switch, interactions
    let currentTheme = 'light';
    let currentState = 'default';

    function toggleTheme() {
      currentTheme = currentTheme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
      document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', currentTheme);
      // Update CSS variables for dark mode
    }

    function setState(state) {
      currentState = state;
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-state]').forEach(el => {
        el.style.display = el.dataset.state === state ? '' : 'none';
      });
    }
  </script>
</body>
</html>
```

### Guidelines ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HTML Preview:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS Variables** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design Tokens (`references/design-tokens.md`) ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° hardcode ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **flexbox/grid** layout (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute position) ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á **class names** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **semantic HTML**: `<header>`, `<main>`, `<nav>`, `<section>`, `<footer>`
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **Google Fonts** (LINE Seed Sans TH) ‚Äî load ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `<link>`
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **inline SVG** ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ placeholder ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö icons/images
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** external CSS frameworks (Bootstrap, Tailwind) ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÜ
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** React, Vue, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ JS framework ‡πÉ‡∏î‡πÜ ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ vanilla JS ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- Animation ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS keyframes** ‡πÉ‡∏ô `<style>` tag
- Keep DOM structure clean ‚Üí clean Figma layer hierarchy

### HTML Best Practices ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HTML to Figma:

| HTML/CSS | Figma Result |
|----------|-------------|
| `display: flex` | Auto Layout |
| `flex-direction: column` | Vertical Auto Layout |
| `gap: 16px` | Item Spacing = 16 |
| `padding: 16px` | Padding = 16 |
| `border-radius: 12px` | Corner Radius = 12 |
| `width: 100%` (‡πÉ‡∏ô flex child) | Layout Sizing = Fill |
| Class name (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô `login-button`) | Layer name = "login-button" |
| Nested `<div>` | Nested frames |

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå: `[screen-name]-preview.html`

---

## Step 4: Iterate ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à (Browser + Claude)

1. **User ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î `.html` ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser** ‚Äî double-click ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Live Preview ‡πÉ‡∏ô VSCode
2. **User ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ú‡∏•** ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å Claude ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô "‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß", "‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° padding", "‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô layout")
3. **Claude ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html`** ‚Üí User refresh browser ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
4. **‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à** ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layout, ‡∏™‡∏µ, ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î, spacing, state ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ
5. ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ: "‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö?"

## Step 5: Import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **html-to-design MCP** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á

### 5.1 ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß

1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ user ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î **html.to.design** plugin ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‚Üí tab **MCP** ‚Üí toggle **"Enable MCP endpoint"** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (STATUS: connected)
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ HTML file ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° import:
   - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox/grid (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ absolute position)
   - Class names ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢
   - ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS Variables
   - DOM structure clean

### 5.2 Import ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô MCP

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_html` ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á:

```
import_html({
  html: "<div class='login-screen'>...</div>",
  css: ".login-screen { display: flex; ... }",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
```

‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ HTML ‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏°‡∏µ external assets ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ serve file ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_url`:

```
import_url({
  url: "http://localhost:3000/login-preview.html",
  name: "Login Screen"
})
```

Plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á HTML ‚Üí Figma layers:
- `display: flex` ‚Üí Auto Layout
- `gap` ‚Üí Item Spacing
- `padding` ‚Üí Padding
- `border-radius` ‚Üí Corner Radius
- Class names ‚Üí Layer names
- Colors ‚Üí Fill colors
- Text ‚Üí Text nodes with font size/weight

### 5.3 Fine-tune ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á import:
1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à Auto Layout structure ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö sizing mode (FILL/HUG/FIXED)
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à font ‚Äî ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô LINE Seed Sans TH ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
3. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à colors ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö HTML preview
4. ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layer names ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
5. ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° components, variants, styles ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£

## Output Files

Skill ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á output ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö step ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà:

| Step | Output | Format |
|------|--------|--------|
| 3 | Interactive Preview | `.html` (Static HTML ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser) |
| 3 | Design Spec Document | `.md` (optional, ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡∏≠) |
| 5 | Figma Design | Import ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô html-to-design MCP (`import_html` / `import_url`) |

## Design Spec Templates

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£ spec ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å preview ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á `.md` ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° template:

### Wireframe (Lo-fi) Template

```markdown
# [Screen Name] ‚Äî Wireframe Specification

## 1. Overview
## 2. Layout Structure (with ASCII wireframe)
## 3. Component List (table)
## 4. Navigation Flow
## 5. UX Principles Applied (table with principle + rationale)
## 6. Notes for Figma Implementation
```

### Hi-fi Template

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Wireframe template + ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°:

```markdown
## 7. Visual Design (Colors, Typography, Spacing, Elevation)
## 8. Design Tokens (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ custom design system)
## 9. Component Specifications (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state: default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled, error)
## 10. Accessibility (contrast, touch targets, VoiceOver/TalkBack labels)
## 11. Responsive Behavior
## 12. Motion & Haptic (iOS)
```

## WCAG Color Contrast Checker (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö)

‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ **‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö WCAG Color Contrast** ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:

### ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô (WCAG 2.1)

| ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó | AA (‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥) | AAA (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥) |
|--------|-------------|-------------|
| Normal text (< 18pt) | 4.5:1 | 7:1 |
| Large text (>= 18pt bold / >= 24pt regular) | 3:1 | 4.5:1 |
| UI components & icons | 3:1 | ‚Äî |

### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Contrast Ratio

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£ relative luminance ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì:

```
Contrast Ratio = (L1 + 0.05) / (L2 + 0.05)
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ L1 = luminance ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤, L2 = luminance ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤

Relative Luminance = 0.2126 * R + 0.7152 * G + 0.0722 * B
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ R, G, B ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô linearization:
  - ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ sRGB <= 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = sRGB / 12.92
  - ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ sRGB > 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = ((sRGB + 0.055) / 1.055) ^ 2.4
```

### ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö (‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á)

1. **‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì contrast ratio ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á text color ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö background color
2. **‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ contrast ratio** ‡πÉ‡∏ô spec ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô: `#F0E8FF on #0D0A14 ‚Üí 15.2:1 ‚úÖ AAA`
3. **‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô AA**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‚Äî ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå
4. **‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á contrast** ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô preview spec info panel

### ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö

```
‚úÖ ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô:
  #F0E8FF on #0D0A14 ‚Üí 15.2:1 (AAA) ‚Äî primary text on dark bg
  #4ADE80 on #0D2818 ‚Üí 6.8:1 (AA)  ‚Äî positive text on green bg

‚ùå ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô:
  #7E6E98 on #1E1830 ‚Üí 2.8:1 (FAIL) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
```

### ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color pair ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç:

- Text on background (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å text level: primary, secondary, tertiary)
- Text on card surfaces
- Text on colored sections (DO/DON'T cards, alerts)
- Icon on background
- Button text on button background
- Placeholder text on input background

---

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ**: ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (px, dp, pt, hex color)
2. **‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á Design Principle**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
3. **Edge Cases**: empty, loading, error, long text, no data
4. **Accessibility First**: contrast ratio, touch target, screen reader
5. **WCAG Contrast Verified**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ text/bg ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô WCAG AA ‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ ratio
6. **Platform-Aware**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û platform conventions
7. **Preview First**: ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π HTML preview ‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
8. **Figma-Ready HTML**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ flexbox/grid, class names ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢, CSS Variables ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° tokens
9. **HTML to Figma MCP**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ html-to-design MCP (`import_html` / `import_url`) ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á
10. **Font ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô HTML**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Google Fonts (LINE Seed Sans TH) ‚Äî font ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á import Figma

# Design Critique / Review Skill

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ feedback ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° UX principles ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠ improvement ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

## Overall Flow

```
1. Capture ‚Üí 2. Read Principles ‚Üí 3. Analyze ‚Üí 4. Score ‚Üí 5. Report ‚Üí 6. Fix (Optional)
```

1. **Capture**: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö design ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (Figma URL, screenshot, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ selection)
2. **Read Principles**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå
3. **Analyze**: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
4. **Score**: ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô
5. **Report**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô report ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° action items
6. **Fix**: ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‚Üí ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô MCP

---

## Step 1: Capture Design

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏):

- **Source**: Figma URL, screenshot path, **HTML preview file (.html)**, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ?
- **Context**: ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£? target user ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£?
- **Platform**: Mobile (iOS/Android), Web, Desktop?
- **Scope**: Review ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á component?
- **Focus Area**: ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design:

**‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma URL:**
```
get_screenshot(fileKey, nodeId)       ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π visual
get_design_context(fileKey, nodeId)   ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design details (‡∏™‡∏µ, font, spacing)
get_metadata(fileKey, nodeId)         ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π structure
get_variable_defs(fileKey, nodeId)    ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π design tokens ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
```

**‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma Selection (TalkToFigma MCP):**
```
read_my_design()                      ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà
get_node_info(nodeId)                 ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î node
scan_text_nodes(nodeId)               ‚Üí scan text ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
scan_nodes_by_types(nodeId, types)    ‚Üí scan components ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° type
```

**‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å HTML Preview File:**
- ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html` preview ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Read tool
- ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå CSS styles, layout structure, colors, typography ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å source code
- ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à contrast, spacing, consistency ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å CSS values ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Principles

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå:

```
references/ux-principles.md        ‚Üí Nielsen's Heuristics + Laws of UX + Gestalt (‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠)
references/material-design.md      ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ Android/Web
references/hig.md                  ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ iOS/macOS
references/design-tokens.md        ‚Üí ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ custom design system
```

---

## Step 3: Analyze ‚Äî ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå 8 ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥

### 3.1 Visual Hierarchy & Layout
- ‡∏°‡∏µ clear hierarchy ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (primary ‚Üí secondary ‚Üí tertiary)
- Information architecture ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Alignment ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ grid consistency
- White space usage ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ?
- Gestalt principles: Proximity, Similarity, Continuity

### 3.2 Typography
- Type scale ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î, ‡∏°‡∏µ hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°)
- Font weight contrast ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Line height / letter spacing ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô font families (‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ, ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 2)

### 3.3 Color & Contrast
- **WCAG Contrast Check** (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö):
  ```
  Contrast Ratio = (L1 + 0.05) / (L2 + 0.05)
  Relative Luminance = 0.2126*R + 0.7152*G + 0.0722*B
  ```
  - Normal text: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
  - Large text (>= 18pt bold / >= 24pt regular): ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 3:1
  - UI components: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 3:1
- Color palette consistency ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ, ‡∏°‡∏µ system ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Semantic color usage ‚Äî error=red, success=green ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Dark mode compatibility (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ)

### 3.4 Component Design
- ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform conventions ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (Jakob's Law)
- Button hierarchy ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (primary, secondary, tertiary)
- Input fields ‡∏°‡∏µ label, placeholder, helper text, error state ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Card/container design consistent ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Interactive elements ‡∏°‡∏µ visual affordance ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.5 Spacing & Consistency
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ spacing system (4px/8px grid) ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Padding/margin consistent ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Component spacing ‡∏°‡∏µ pattern ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.6 UX Heuristics (Nielsen's 10)
‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠:
- H1: Visibility of System Status ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ feedback ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H2: Match Real World ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H3: User Control ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö/undo ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H4: Consistency ‚Äî follow platform standards ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H5: Error Prevention ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô error ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H6: Recognition > Recall ‚Äî ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H7: Flexibility ‚Äî ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö novice & expert ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H8: Aesthetic & Minimalist ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H9: Error Recovery ‚Äî error message ‡∏î‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- H10: Help & Documentation ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ guidance ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

### 3.7 Accessibility
- Touch targets >= 44pt (iOS) / 48dp (Android)?
- Color not the only indicator?
- Screen reader friendly? (labels, roles)
- Sufficient contrast? (checked in 3.3)

### 3.8 Edge Cases
- Empty state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Loading state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Error state ‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- Long text / overflow handling?
- No data / no results state?

---

## Step 4: Score ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô

### Scoring Matrix

| ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ | Weight | ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô (1-10) | ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏ |
|------|--------|-------------|----------|
| Visual Hierarchy & Layout | 15% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Typography | 10% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Color & Contrast | 15% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Component Design | 15% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Spacing & Consistency | 10% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| UX Heuristics | 20% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Accessibility | 10% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Edge Cases | 5% | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| **Weighted Total** | **100%** | **‚Äî/10** | ‚Äî |

### Rating Scale
- **9-10**: World-class ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£
- **7-8**: ‡∏î‡∏µ ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ minor improvements
- **5-6**: ‡∏õ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- **3-4**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á ‚Äî ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô
- **1-2**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á redesign ‚Äî ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏á

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

# User Flow / Information Architecture Skill

‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö User Flow ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Information Architecture ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö app/web ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á journey

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read Principles ‚Üí 3. Map IA ‚Üí 4. Design Flows ‚Üí 5. Generate Diagrams ‚Üí 6. Build in Figma (Optional)
```

1. **Requirements**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à product, users, features
2. **Read Principles**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô UX + navigation patterns
3. **Map IA**: ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á Information Architecture
4. **Design Flows**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á user flows ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö key tasks
5. **Generate Diagrams**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á diagram ‡πÉ‡∏ô FigJam/Figma
6. **Build in Figma**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (optional)

> **‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠**: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ flow ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ **figma-ui-design-spec** skill ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏):

- **Product**: ‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏õ/‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£? ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **Target Users**: ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (1-3 personas)
- **Platform**: Mobile (iOS/Android), Web, Desktop, Cross-platform?
- **Key Features**: features ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ (list ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤)
- **User Goals**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à? (top 3-5 goals)
- **Scope**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á module?
- **Reference**: ‡∏°‡∏µ app ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô reference ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Design Principles

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô reference files:

```
references/ux-principles.md        ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠ (‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Hick's Law, Miller's Law, Jakob's Law)
references/material-design.md      ‚Üí Navigation patterns ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Android/Web
references/hig.md                  ‚Üí Navigation patterns ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö iOS
```

### Navigation Patterns ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ:

**iOS (HIG):**
- Tab Bar (3-5 items) + Navigation Stack ‚Äî most common
- Sidebar (iPad) ‚Üí Tab Bar (iPhone)
- Modal Sheets ‚Äî focused tasks

**Android (Material):**
- Bottom Navigation (3-5 items) ‚Äî compact
- Navigation Rail ‚Äî medium screens
- Navigation Drawer ‚Äî expanded screens

**Web:**
- Top Navigation Bar + Side Navigation
- Breadcrumbs for deep hierarchy
- Tab-based navigation for related content

## Step 3: Map Information Architecture

### 3.1 Feature Inventory

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° features ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô categories:

```markdown
## Feature Inventory

| Category | Features | Priority |
|----------|----------|----------|
| Authentication | Login, Register, Forgot Password, Social Login | Must Have |
| Profile | View Profile, Edit Profile, Settings | Must Have |
| [Core Feature] | [list features] | Must Have |
| [Secondary] | [list features] | Should Have |
| [Nice-to-have] | [list features] | Could Have |
```

### 3.2 Content Model

‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î entities ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ relationships:

```markdown
## Content Model

| Entity | Key Attributes | Relationships |
|--------|---------------|---------------|
| User | name, email, avatar, role | has many Posts, has many Orders |
| Product | title, price, image, category | belongs to Category, has many Reviews |
| Order | items, total, status, date | belongs to User, has many Products |
```

### 3.3 Site Map / Screen Map

‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î hierarchy ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á screens:

```markdown
## Screen Map

### Level 0: Entry
- Splash / Onboarding

### Level 1: Main Navigation (Tab Bar / Bottom Nav)
- Home (Tab 1)
- Search (Tab 2)
- [Core Feature] (Tab 3)
- Profile (Tab 4)

### Level 2: Sub-screens
- Home ‚Üí Product Detail
- Home ‚Üí Category List ‚Üí Product List
- Search ‚Üí Search Results ‚Üí Product Detail
- Profile ‚Üí Settings ‚Üí Edit Profile
- Profile ‚Üí Order History ‚Üí Order Detail

### Level 3: Modals / Overlays
- Cart Sheet
- Filter Sheet
- Login Modal
```

### 3.4 Navigation Matrix

```markdown
## Navigation Matrix

| From \ To | Home | Search | Detail | Cart | Profile |
|-----------|------|--------|--------|------|---------|
| Home | ‚Äî | Tab | Push | Sheet | Tab |
| Search | Tab | ‚Äî | Push | Sheet | Tab |
| Detail | Back | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | Sheet | ‚Äî |
| Cart | Dismiss | ‚Äî | Push | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |
| Profile | Tab | Tab | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | ‚Äî |

Transition types: Tab (tab switch), Push (nav push), Sheet (modal), Back (pop), Dismiss (close modal)
```
