## Step 4: Design User Flows

### 4.1 Identify Key Flows

‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å top 3-5 flows ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î:

```markdown
## Key User Flows

| # | Flow Name | User Goal | Priority | Complexity |
|---|-----------|-----------|----------|------------|
| 1 | Onboarding | ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô | Critical | Medium |
| 2 | [Core Task] | [goal] | Critical | High |
| 3 | Purchase | ‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à | Critical | High |
| 4 | Search & Filter | ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ | High | Medium |
| 5 | Account Management | ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ | Medium | Low |
```

### 4.2 Flow Diagram Format

‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ flow ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ format ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

```markdown
### Flow: [Flow Name]

**User Goal**: [‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£]
**Entry Point**: [‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô]
**Success State**: [‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£]
**Happy Path Steps**: [‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô steps]

#### Happy Path:
1. [Screen A] ‚Üí User action: [action] ‚Üí
2. [Screen B] ‚Üí User action: [action] ‚Üí
3. [Screen C] ‚Üí Success ‚úì

#### Error/Alternative Paths:
- Step 2 error: [validation fail] ‚Üí Show inline error ‚Üí Retry
- Step 2 alternative: [‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏î back] ‚Üí Return to Screen A
- Step 3 timeout: [network error] ‚Üí Error state ‚Üí Retry button

#### Decision Points:
- [Screen B]: if logged in ‚Üí skip to Step 3; if not ‚Üí show login modal
- [Screen C]: if first time ‚Üí show tutorial; if returning ‚Üí skip

#### Edge Cases:
- No network ‚Üí Offline state with cached data
- Session expired ‚Üí Re-auth modal
- Deep link entry ‚Üí Skip to Step 2 with prefilled data
```

### 4.3 Flow Principles

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å flow ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£:

- **Hick's Law**: ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ step ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 5-7
- **Miller's Law**: ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 7¬±2 chunks
- **Doherty Threshold**: ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ transition ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á < 400ms (perceived)
- **H1 - Visibility**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà step ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á flow
- **H3 - User Control**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å step ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö/undo
- **H5 - Error Prevention**: ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô error ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô submit

---

## Step 5: Generate Diagrams

### 5.1 ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Flow Diagram (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Figma Remote MCP)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `generate_diagram` ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Mermaid.js diagram:

```
generate_diagram({
  name: "User Registration Flow",
  mermaidSyntax: 'flowchart LR\n  A["Splash Screen"] -->|"Tap Get Started"| B["Sign Up Form"]\n  B -->|"Fill & Submit"| C{"Valid?"}\n  C -->|"Yes"| D["Verify Email"]\n  C -->|"No"| B\n  D -->|"Code Entered"| E["Welcome Screen"]\n  E -->|"Continue"| F["Home"]',
  userIntent: "Registration user flow diagram"
})
```

### Diagram Types ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ:

| Type | Mermaid Syntax | Use Case |
|------|---------------|----------|
| Flowchart | `flowchart LR` | User flows, task flows |
| Sequence | `sequenceDiagram` | API interactions, system flows |
| State Diagram | `stateDiagram-v2` | Screen states, component states |
| Gantt | `gantt` | Project timeline, feature roadmap |

### 5.2 Flow Diagram Best Practices

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `flowchart LR` (left-to-right) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö user flows
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `flowchart TD` (top-down) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö decision trees
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å node ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ label ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏û‡∏π‡∏î
- Decision points ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ rhombus `{"Decision?"}`
- Color coding: green=success, red=error, blue=action
- ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ emoji ‡πÉ‡∏ô Mermaid syntax

### 5.3 Screen Map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma (Optional ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ TalkToFigma MCP)

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á visual screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:

```
1. ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á frame ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen (create_frame with name)
2. ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ screen (create_text)
3. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ create_connections ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏° screens
4. ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î layout ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° hierarchy
```

## Step 6: Build Screen Map in Figma (Optional)

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ screen map ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:

### 6.1 Screen Card Template

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á card ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ screen:
```
create_frame({
  name: "Screen: Home",
  x, y, width: 200, height: 120,
  fillColor: { r: 0.95, g: 0.95, b: 1 },
  layoutMode: "VERTICAL",
  itemSpacing: 8,
  paddingTop: 12, paddingBottom: 12, paddingLeft: 16, paddingRight: 16
})
```

### 6.2 Connect Screens

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `create_connections` ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°:
```
create_connections({
  connections: [
    { startNodeId: "home-id", endNodeId: "detail-id", text: "Tap Product" },
    { startNodeId: "home-id", endNodeId: "search-id", text: "Tab Switch" }
  ]
})
```

### 6.3 Annotate

‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà annotations ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ flow logic:
```
set_multiple_annotations({
  nodeId: "flow-frame-id",
  annotations: [
    { nodeId: "decision-id", labelMarkdown: "**Decision**\nIf logged in ‚Üí skip auth" }
  ]
})
```

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **Goal-Oriented**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å user goal ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà feature list
2. **Happy Path First**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö happy path ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î edge cases
3. **Minimal Steps**: ‡∏•‡∏î steps ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î (3-click rule ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô guideline)
4. **Clear Wayfinding**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
5. **Consistent Navigation**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ pattern ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app
6. **Error Recovery**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å flow ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ error handling
7. **Platform Conventions**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ navigation patterns ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform

# Accessibility Audit Skill

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Accessibility ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° WCAG 2.1 AA/AAA ‚Äî ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ

## Overall Flow

```
1. Capture ‚Üí 2. Read Guidelines ‚Üí 3. Audit (7 Categories) ‚Üí 4. Score ‚Üí 5. Report ‚Üí 6. Fix
```

---

## Step 1: Capture Design

‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô Design Critique skill:

- **Figma URL** ‚Üí `get_screenshot`, `get_design_context`, `get_metadata`
- **Figma Selection** ‚Üí `read_my_design`, `scan_text_nodes`, `scan_nodes_by_types`
- **HTML Preview File** ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html` ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Read tool ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à contrast, touch targets, semantic HTML, ARIA attributes ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å source code ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á (‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô import Figma)
- **Context**: ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ target WCAG level ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ AA ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ AAA?

---

## Step 2: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Guidelines

```
references/ux-principles.md     ‚Üí Accessibility sections
references/hig.md               ‚Üí iOS Accessibility guidelines
references/material-design.md   ‚Üí Material Accessibility guidelines
```

---

## Step 3: Audit ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à 7 ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î

### Category 1: Color Contrast (WCAG 1.4.3 / 1.4.6)

**‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì Contrast Ratio:**
```
Contrast Ratio = (L1 + 0.05) / (L2 + 0.05)

Relative Luminance = 0.2126*R + 0.7152*G + 0.0722*B
‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ R, G, B linearized:
  sRGB <= 0.03928 ‚Üí linear = sRGB / 12.92
  sRGB > 0.03928  ‚Üí linear = ((sRGB + 0.055) / 1.055) ^ 2.4
```

**‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå:**

| Element | AA (‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥) | AAA (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥) |
|---------|-------------|-------------|
| Normal text (< 18pt / < 14pt bold) | 4.5:1 | 7:1 |
| Large text (>= 18pt / >= 14pt bold) | 3:1 | 4.5:1 |
| UI components & icons | 3:1 | ‚Äî |
| Non-text contrast (borders, inputs) | 3:1 | ‚Äî |

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ:**
- Text on background (primary, secondary, tertiary, disabled)
- Text on cards / colored surfaces
- Text on images (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ overlay)
- Icon on background
- Button text on button fill
- Placeholder text on input background
- Link text vs surrounding text
- Focus indicator contrast
- Border / divider visibility

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Foreground | Background | Ratio | Size | AA | AAA |
|---------|-----------|------------|-------|------|----|-----|
| Body text | #1A1A1A | #FFFFFF | 16.6:1 | 14px | PASS | PASS |
| Secondary text | #666666 | #FFFFFF | 5.7:1 | 14px | PASS | FAIL |
| Button label | #FFFFFF | #007AFF | 4.6:1 | 14pt bold | PASS | PASS |
| Placeholder | #999999 | #F5F5F5 | 2.1:1 | 14px | FAIL | FAIL |
```

### Category 2: Touch Targets (WCAG 2.5.5 / 2.5.8)

**‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå:**

| Platform | Minimum Size | Recommended | Spacing |
|----------|-------------|-------------|---------|
| iOS | 44 x 44pt | 56 x 56pt (primary) | >= 8pt |
| Android | 48 x 48dp | 56 x 56dp (primary) | >= 8dp |
| Web | 44 x 44px (WCAG) | 48 x 48px | >= 8px |

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å button, link, icon button, toggle, checkbox, radio
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element ‡πÉ‡∏ô list (row tap area)
- Close buttons, back buttons
- Form elements (input tap area, dropdown)
- Navigation items (tab bar, nav bar buttons)

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Actual Size | Min Required | Status | Note |
|---------|------------|--------------|--------|------|
| Back button | 44x44pt | 44x44pt | PASS | ‚Äî |
| Star rating icon | 24x24pt | 44x44pt | FAIL | Add padding to 44pt |
| List row | 44pt height | 44pt | PASS | Full-width tap area |
```

### Category 3: Screen Reader / Assistive Technology (WCAG 1.1.1 / 4.1.2)

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**

| Check | Description | How to verify |
|-------|-------------|---------------|
| Image alt text | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å meaningful image ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ alt text | ‡∏î‡∏π image nodes |
| Decorative images | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á hide ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å screen reader | ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô decorative ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏° |
| Button labels | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å button ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ accessible label | ‡∏î‡∏π text content |
| Icon-only buttons | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ accessibilityLabel | ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πá‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ visible label ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ aria-label |
| Form labels | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å input ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á associate ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö label | ‡∏î‡∏π label-input relationship |
| Heading structure | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ proper heading hierarchy (h1‚Üíh2‚Üíh3) | ‡∏î‡∏π text hierarchy |
| Reading order | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà make sense | ‡∏î‡∏π visual order vs DOM order |
| Focus order | tab order ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á logical | ‡∏î‡∏π interactive element order |
| Link purpose | link text ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "click here") | ‡∏î‡∏π link text |
| Error announcements | error ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á announce ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ screen reader | ‡∏î‡∏π error handling |

**Output Table:**
```markdown
| Element | Check | Status | Issue | Fix |
|---------|-------|--------|-------|-----|
| Search icon | Label | FAIL | No accessible label | Add "Search" label |
| Hero image | Alt text | FAIL | Missing alt | Add descriptive alt |
| Email field | Form label | PASS | Has visible label | ‚Äî |
| "Click here" link | Link purpose | FAIL | Vague text | Change to "View pricing" |
```

### Category 4: Color Independence (WCAG 1.4.1)

‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß:

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
- Error states: ‡∏°‡∏µ icon ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ text ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏î‡∏á?
- Success states: ‡∏°‡∏µ checkmark ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß?
- Required fields: ‡∏°‡∏µ * ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Active/selected states: ‡∏°‡∏µ indicator ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Charts/graphs: ‡∏°‡∏µ pattern/label ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?
- Links in text: ‡∏°‡∏µ underline ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≤?
- Status badges: ‡∏°‡∏µ icon + text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏™‡∏µ?

**Color Blindness Simulation:**

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ design ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö color vision deficiencies:
- Protanopia (red-blind, ~1% males)
- Deuteranopia (green-blind, ~1% males)
- Tritanopia (blue-blind, rare)
- Achromatopsia (total color blind, very rare)

‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á:
- Red vs Green (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô error vs success) ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ shape/icon ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢
- Red vs Brown, Green vs Brown
- Blue vs Purple
- Light Green vs Light Yellow

### Category 5: Keyboard Navigation (WCAG 2.1.1 / 2.1.2 / 2.4.7)

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Web / Desktop:

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
| Check | Description |
|-------|-------------|
| All interactive reachable | ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å interactive element ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á tab ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ |
| Focus visible | focus indicator ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î (contrast >= 3:1) |
| Focus order | tab order logical ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° visual layout |
| No keyboard trap | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å element ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (especially modals) |
| Skip links | ‡∏°‡∏µ "Skip to main content" link |
| Shortcuts | keyboard shortcuts ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà conflict ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö screen reader |
| Modal focus trap | focus ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á trap ‡πÉ‡∏ô modal ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î |

**Focus Indicator Style:**
```
Focus ring: 2px solid, contrast >= 3:1 vs background AND focused element
Recommended: #005FCC (blue) on light, #66B2FF on dark
Offset: 2px from element edge
```

### Category 6: Text & Readability (WCAG 1.4.4 / 1.4.8 / 1.4.12)

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
| Check | Criteria |
|-------|----------|
| Text resize | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö zoom 200% ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢ content |
| Line height | >= 1.5x font size ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö body text |
| Paragraph spacing | >= 2x font size |
| Letter spacing | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á adjust ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà lock ‡πÉ‡∏ô image) |
| Text alignment | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà justify (justified text ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å) |
| Line length | 45-75 characters per line (optimal: 66) |
| Font size minimum | >= 16px/16sp/16pt ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö body text |
| Dynamic Type (iOS) | ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Dynamic Type scaling |
| Text in images | ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ real text ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô |

### Category 7: Motion & Cognitive (WCAG 2.3.1 / 2.3.3)

**‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à:**
| Check | Criteria |
|-------|----------|
| Reduce Motion | ‡∏°‡∏µ alternative ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Reduce Motion ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î? |
| Auto-play | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà auto-play video/animation > 5 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ |
| Flashing | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ content flash > 3 ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ |
| Parallax | ‡∏•‡∏î‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Reduce Motion |
| Timeout | ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô session timeout |
| Cognitive load | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ |
| Plain language | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô |
| Consistent layout | layout consistent ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app |
| Error recovery | ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ recover ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å error |
| Predictable | interactions ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á |

# Design System Creation Skill

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Design System ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö ‚Äî ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà tokens, typography scale, color system, components ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á documentation ‚Äî ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read References ‚Üí 3. Define Foundations ‚Üí 4. Design Components ‚Üí 5. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 6. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP) ‚Üí 7. Document
```

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Brand**: ‡∏°‡∏µ brand guidelines ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? (‡∏™‡∏µ, font, logo)
- **Platform**: Mobile, Web, Cross-platform?
- **Base System**: ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Material Design / HIG / ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå?
- **Scale**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ô? ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà product? (‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ã‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô)
- **Components Needed**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ components ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á? (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥?)
- **Theme**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Light/Dark mode ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?

## Step 3: Define Foundations (Design Tokens)

### 3.1 Color System

**Step-by-step:**

1. **‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å Primary Color** ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å brand (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà)
2. **Generate Color Scale** ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ hue:
   ```
   [color]-50:  lightest (background tint)
   [color]-100: very light
   [color]-200: light
   [color]-300: medium light
   [color]-400: medium
   [color]-500: base (primary)
   [color]-600: medium dark
   [color]-700: dark
   [color]-800: very dark
   [color]-900: darkest
   [color]-950: near black
   ```

3. **‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Semantic Colors**:
   ```markdown
   | Token | Light Mode | Dark Mode | Usage |
   |-------|-----------|-----------|-------|
   | color-primary | blue-600 | blue-400 | Primary actions, links |
   | color-on-primary | white | blue-950 | Text on primary |
   | color-secondary | gray-600 | gray-400 | Secondary actions |
   | color-error | red-600 | red-400 | Error states |
   | color-warning | amber-600 | amber-400 | Warning states |
   | color-success | green-600 | green-400 | Success states |
   | color-info | blue-500 | blue-300 | Informational |
   | color-surface | white | gray-900 | Backgrounds |
   | color-on-surface | gray-900 | gray-50 | Primary text |
   | color-on-surface-variant | gray-600 | gray-400 | Secondary text |
   | color-outline | gray-300 | gray-700 | Borders |
   | color-outline-variant | gray-200 | gray-800 | Subtle borders |
   ```

4. **WCAG Contrast Check** (‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö):
   ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏π‡πà semantic color:
   ```
   color-on-surface on color-surface ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   color-on-primary on color-primary ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   color-on-surface-variant on color-surface ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á >= 4.5:1 (AA)
   ```

### 3.2 Typography Scale

**‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Type Scale:**

```markdown
| Token | Size | Weight | Line Height | Letter Spacing | Usage |
|-------|------|--------|-------------|----------------|-------|
| display-lg | 57px | 400 | 64px | -0.25px | Hero text |
| display-md | 45px | 400 | 52px | 0 | Page hero |
| display-sm | 36px | 400 | 44px | 0 | Section hero |
| heading-lg | 32px | 700 | 40px | 0 | Page title |
| heading-md | 24px | 700 | 32px | 0 | Section title |
| heading-sm | 20px | 600 | 28px | 0 | Card title |
| title-lg | 18px | 600 | 28px | 0 | Subtitle |
| title-md | 16px | 500 | 24px | 0.15px | List title |
| title-sm | 14px | 500 | 20px | 0.1px | Small title |
| body-lg | 16px | 400 | 24px | 0.5px | Primary body |
| body-md | 14px | 400 | 20px | 0.25px | Secondary body |
| body-sm | 12px | 400 | 16px | 0.4px | Caption |
| label-lg | 14px | 500 | 20px | 0.1px | Button label |
| label-md | 12px | 500 | 16px | 0.5px | Tab label |
| label-sm | 11px | 500 | 16px | 0.5px | Badge label |
```

**Font Family:**
- Primary: [brand font or system font]
- Mono: [monospace font for code/data]
- ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ fallback stack ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠

### 3.3 Spacing System

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ 4px base unit:

```markdown
| Token | Value | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| space-0 | 0px | ‚Äî |
| space-1 | 4px | Icon padding, micro gaps |
| space-2 | 8px | Inline elements, tight |
| space-3 | 12px | List item internal |
| space-4 | 16px | Content padding (default) |
| space-5 | 20px | Card padding |
| space-6 | 24px | Section gaps |
| space-8 | 32px | Large gaps |
| space-10 | 40px | Section breaks |
| space-12 | 48px | Page sections |
| space-16 | 64px | Hero spacing |
| space-20 | 80px | Page top/bottom |
```

### 3.4 Shape (Corner Radius)

```markdown
| Token | Value | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| radius-none | 0px | Sharp corners |
| radius-xs | 4px | Tags, badges, chips |
| radius-sm | 8px | Buttons, inputs, small cards |
| radius-md | 12px | Cards, dialogs |
| radius-lg | 16px | Large cards, FABs |
| radius-xl | 24px | Bottom sheets |
| radius-full | 9999px | Pills, avatars, circles |
```

### 3.5 Elevation

```markdown
| Token | Shadow | Usage |
|-------|--------|-------|
| elevation-0 | none | Flat surfaces |
| elevation-1 | 0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.12) | Cards (rest) |
| elevation-2 | 0 4px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.1) | Dropdowns, popovers |
| elevation-3 | 0 8px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.1) | FAB, bottom sheets |
| elevation-4 | 0 12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.12) | Dialogs, modals |
```

## Step 4: Design Components

### Atomic Design Hierarchy

```
Atoms ‚Üí Molecules ‚Üí Organisms ‚Üí Templates ‚Üí Pages
```

### 4.1 Atoms (‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô)

| Component | Variants | States |
|-----------|----------|--------|
| Button | filled, outlined, text, tonal, icon | default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled, loading |
| Icon Button | filled, outlined, standard | default, hover, pressed, focused, disabled |
| Text Field | filled, outlined | default, focused, filled, error, disabled |
| Checkbox | ‚Äî | unchecked, checked, indeterminate, disabled |
| Radio Button | ‚Äî | unselected, selected, disabled |
| Toggle/Switch | ‚Äî | off, on, disabled |
| Badge | number, dot | ‚Äî |
| Chip | assist, filter, input, suggestion | default, selected, disabled |
| Divider | full-width, inset | ‚Äî |
| Avatar | image, initials, icon | sizes: sm, md, lg |

### 4.2 Molecules (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å atoms)

| Component | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| Search Bar | input + icon + clear button |
| List Item | avatar + text + trailing action |
| Form Field | label + input + helper text + error text |
| Menu Item | icon + label + shortcut |
| Snackbar / Toast | text + optional action button |
| Tab | icon + label + indicator |

### 4.3 Organisms (complex components)

| Component | Description |
|-----------|-------------|
| Top App Bar | nav icon + title + action icons |
| Bottom Navigation | 3-5 tab items |
| Navigation Rail | icon + label items |
| Navigation Drawer | header + menu items |
| Card | header + content + actions |
| Dialog / Modal | title + body + action buttons |
| Bottom Sheet | handle + content |
| Data Table | header + rows + pagination |
| Form | grouped form fields + submit |

### Component Spec Template

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ component ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î:

```markdown
## Component: [Name]

### Anatomy
[‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ sub-elements]

### Variants
| Variant | Visual Difference | When to Use |
|---------|------------------|-------------|
| Filled | Solid background | Primary actions |
| Outlined | Border only | Secondary actions |

### Sizes
| Size | Height | Padding | Font | Icon |
|------|--------|---------|------|------|
| Small | 32px | 12px H | label-md | 16px |
| Medium | 40px | 16px H | label-lg | 20px |
| Large | 48px | 20px H | body-lg | 24px |

### States
| State | Background | Text | Border | Opacity |
|-------|-----------|------|--------|---------|
| Default | primary | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Hover | primary-dark | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Pressed | primary-darker | on-primary | ‚Äî | 100% |
| Focused | primary | on-primary | focus-ring | 100% |
| Disabled | on-surface | on-surface | ‚Äî | 38% |
| Loading | primary | ‚Äî | ‚Äî | 70% + spinner |

### Accessibility
- Min touch target: 48x48dp / 44x44pt
- Focus indicator: 2px ring
- Disabled: opacity 38%, not focusable
- Screen reader: role="button", aria-label if icon-only

### Spacing Rules
- Internal padding: [values]
- Min gap between buttons: space-2 (8px)
- Margin from screen edge: space-4 (16px)
```

## Step 5: Preview (Static HTML)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á Design System Overview ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ:

### Preview ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:

1. **Color Palette** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color token ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° hex (CSS Variables)
2. **Typography Scale** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å type style (Google Fonts: LINE Seed Sans TH)
3. **Spacing Scale** ‚Äî visual representation
4. **Component Gallery** ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component, ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å variant, ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state
5. **Light/Dark Toggle** ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö theme ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)
6. **Component State Switcher** ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô state ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)

### Guidelines:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS Variables** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design Tokens (`references/design-tokens.md`)
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **flexbox/grid** layout ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á **class names** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‚Üí ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Figma layer names
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **semantic HTML** (`<header>`, `<section>`, `<main>`)
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** React, Vue, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ JS framework ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ vanilla JS ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **inline SVG** ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ placeholder ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö icons

‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: `[system-name]-design-system-preview.html`

   ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ serve file ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_url`:

   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à font ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô LINE Seed Sans TH ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à sizing mode (FILL/HUG/FIXED)

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **Token-First**: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î tokens ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö component
2. **Consistent Naming**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `{category}-{property}-{variant}` ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠
3. **Scalable**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° variant/component ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
4. **Accessible by Default**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô WCAG AA
5. **Theme-Ready**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å color token ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ Light + Dark mode
6. **Platform-Aware**: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö sizing/spacing ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° platform (pt vs dp vs px)
7. **Document Everything**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å component ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ usage guideline
8. **Less is More**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å minimal set ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°

# Responsive / Adaptive Design Skill

‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö UI ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠ ‚Äî ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Mobile ‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏ô Desktop ‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ frames ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma

## Overall Flow

```
1. Requirements ‚Üí 2. Read References ‚Üí 3. Define Breakpoints ‚Üí 4. Design Adaptation Rules ‚Üí 5. Preview (HTML) ‚Üí 6. Import to Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)
```

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Requirements

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

- **Primary Platform**: Mobile-first ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Desktop-first?
- **Target Breakpoints**: ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î? (Mobile / Tablet / Desktop / Large Desktop)
- **Screen/Feature**: ‡∏à‡∏∞ responsive ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£? (‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß / ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app)
- **Content Priority**: content ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile?
- **Navigation**: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô navigation pattern ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° size ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (size ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß) ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Framework**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS framework ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô? (Tailwind, Bootstrap, custom)

## Step 3: Define Breakpoints

### 3.1 Standard Breakpoints

| Breakpoint | Width | Device Category | Columns | Margin | Gutter |
|------------|-------|----------------|---------|--------|--------|
| xs | < 360px | Small phone | 4 | 16px | 8px |
| sm | 360-599px | Phone | 4 | 16px | 8px |
| md | 600-904px | Tablet portrait / Foldable | 8 | 24px | 16px |
| lg | 905-1239px | Tablet landscape / Small desktop | 12 | 24px | 24px |
| xl | 1240-1439px | Desktop | 12 | 24px | 24px |
| 2xl | >= 1440px | Large desktop | 12 | auto (max-width) | 24px |

### 3.2 Common Frame Sizes ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Figma

| Device | Width | Height | Use For |
|--------|-------|--------|---------|
| iPhone SE | 375px | 667px | Small phone |
| iPhone 15 Pro | 393px | 852px | Standard phone |
| iPhone 15 Pro Max | 430px | 932px | Large phone |
| iPad Mini | 744px | 1133px | Small tablet |
| iPad Pro 11" | 834px | 1194px | Tablet |
| iPad Pro 12.9" | 1024px | 1366px | Large tablet |
| MacBook Air | 1440px | 900px | Desktop |
| Desktop HD | 1920px | 1080px | Large desktop |

### 3.3 ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å Target Sizes

**Minimum recommended (3 sizes):**
```
Mobile:  393 x 852px   (iPhone 15 Pro)
Tablet:  834 x 1194px  (iPad Pro 11")
Desktop: 1440 x 900px  (MacBook Air)
```

**Comprehensive (5 sizes):**
```
Small Phone:  375 x 667px
Phone:        393 x 852px
Tablet:       834 x 1194px
Desktop:      1440 x 900px
Large Desktop: 1920 x 1080px
```

## Step 4: Design Adaptation Rules

### 4.1 Layout Adaptation Strategies

| Strategy | Description | Example |
|----------|-------------|---------|
| **Reflow** | Stack ‚Üí Row | Cards stack vertical on mobile, horizontal on desktop |
| **Expand** | ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° width | Sidebar ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å icon-only ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô full-width |
| **Reveal** | Show more content | ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á sidebar ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile |
| **Hide** | ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô non-essential | ‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô secondary info ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile |
| **Resize** | ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î | Image full-width ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile, fixed width ‡∏ö‡∏ô desktop |
| **Reposition** | ‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á | FAB ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile ‚Üí inline button ‡∏ö‡∏ô desktop |
| **Transform** | ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô component | Bottom sheet ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile ‚Üí side panel ‡∏ö‡∏ô desktop |

### 4.2 Navigation Adaptation

| Size | Primary Nav | Secondary Nav |
|------|-------------|---------------|
| Mobile (< 600) | Bottom Tab Bar (3-5 items) | Hamburger ‚Üí Drawer |
| Tablet (600-904) | Navigation Rail (side icons) | Tab bar |
| Desktop (905+) | Sidebar Navigation (full) | Top tabs |

### 4.3 Content Adaptation Rules

‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ section ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î:

```markdown
## Content Adaptation

### Hero Section
| Breakpoint | Layout | Image | Text |
|------------|--------|-------|------|
| Mobile | Stack (image top, text bottom) | Full-width, 16:9 | heading-md, body-md |
| Tablet | Side-by-side (50/50) | 1:1 | heading-lg, body-lg |
| Desktop | Side-by-side (40/60) | Custom crop | display-sm, body-lg |

### Card Grid
| Breakpoint | Columns | Card Width | Gap |
|------------|---------|------------|-----|
| Mobile | 1 | 100% | 16px |
| Tablet | 2 | calc(50% - 12px) | 24px |
| Desktop | 3-4 | calc(33% - 16px) | 24px |

### Data Table
| Breakpoint | Adaptation |
|------------|------------|
| Mobile | Transform to card list (stack rows) |
| Tablet | Horizontal scroll with sticky first column |
| Desktop | Full table view |

### Form Layout
| Breakpoint | Columns | Input Width |
|------------|---------|-------------|
| Mobile | 1 | 100% |
| Tablet | 2 (side-by-side for short fields) | 50% |
| Desktop | 2-3 | 33-50% |
```

### 4.4 Typography Adaptation

```markdown
## Typography Scale by Breakpoint

| Token | Mobile | Tablet | Desktop |
|-------|--------|--------|---------|
| display | 36px | 45px | 57px |
| heading-lg | 24px | 28px | 32px |
| heading-md | 20px | 22px | 24px |
| body | 16px | 16px | 16px |
| body-sm | 14px | 14px | 14px |
```

Body text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô headings/display scale ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠

### 4.5 Spacing Adaptation

```markdown
## Spacing by Breakpoint

| Token | Mobile | Tablet | Desktop |
|-------|--------|--------|---------|
| page-margin | 16px | 24px | 24px (or auto center) |
| section-gap | 24px | 32px | 48px |
| card-padding | 16px | 20px | 24px |
| content-padding | 16px | 24px | 24px |
```

### 4.6 Touch Target Adaptation

| Breakpoint | Min Target | Reason |
|------------|-----------|--------|
| Mobile | 48 x 48px | Touch (finger) |
| Tablet | 44 x 44px | Touch + stylus |
| Desktop | 32 x 32px (click) | Mouse (but keep 44px accessible) |

---

## Step 5: Preview (Static HTML)

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà **resize ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ** ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô browser ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å resize ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ:

### Preview ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ:

1. **Responsive Container** ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ CSS `resize: horizontal` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö breakpoint (vanilla JS)
2. **Breakpoint Indicator** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á current breakpoint (xs/sm/md/lg/xl) ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ vanilla JS + `matchMedia()`
3. **Side-by-side View** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á Mobile + Tablet + Desktop ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `<iframe>` ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ CSS Grid)
4. **Layout Annotations** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á grid columns, margins, gaps
5. **Light/Dark Toggle** ‚Äî ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö theme ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (vanilla JS)
6. **Content Priority Highlight** ‚Äî ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ content ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢/‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ resize

### Guidelines:

- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS media queries** (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ container queries) ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á
- ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á breakpoint badge ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢
- ‡∏°‡∏µ ruler/grid overlay toggle (vanilla JS)
- ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å adaptation rule ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ resize
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **CSS Variables** ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Design Tokens (`references/design-tokens.md`)
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **flexbox/grid** layout ‚Üí Auto Layout ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma
- **‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** React, Vue, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ JS framework ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ vanilla JS ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô

‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠: `[screen-name]-responsive-preview.html`

---

## Step 6: Import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma (HTML to Figma MCP)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ **html-to-design MCP** ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á:

1. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ user ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î html.to.design plugin ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma ‚Üí tab MCP ‚Üí STATUS: connected
2. ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_html` ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á HTML ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ breakpoint ‡πÑ‡∏õ Figma:
   ```
   import_html({ html: "...", css: "...", name: "Login - Mobile (393px)" })
   import_html({ html: "...", css: "...", name: "Login - Tablet (834px)" })
   import_html({ html: "...", css: "...", name: "Login - Desktop (1440px)" })
   ```
   ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ serve file ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `import_url`:
   ```
   import_url({ url: "http://localhost:3000/login-responsive-preview.html", name: "Login Responsive" })
   ```
3. Plugin ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á HTML ‚Üí Figma layers ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
4. ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö fine-tune ‡πÉ‡∏ô Figma:
   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à font ‚Äî ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô LINE Seed Sans TH ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
   - ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à sizing mode (FILL/HUG/FIXED)
   - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö layer names ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
   - ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î frames ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° breakpoint (Mobile ‚Üí Tablet ‚Üí Desktop)

---

## Responsive Design Checklist

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö:

### Layout
- [ ] ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å breakpoint ‡∏°‡∏µ consistent visual identity
- [ ] Content priority ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô)
- [ ] Grid system consistent (columns, margins, gutters)
- [ ] Max-width ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö large screens (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà stretch ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å)
- [ ] Line length ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 75 characters

### Navigation
- [ ] Navigation pattern ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö screen size
- [ ] Navigation transitions smooth (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà jump)
- [ ] ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å page reachable ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å breakpoint

### Typography
- [ ] Display/heading sizes scale ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° breakpoint
- [ ] Body text readable (>= 16px) ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å size
- [ ] Line height comfortable ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å size

### Touch & Interaction
- [ ] Touch targets >= 48px ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile/tablet
- [ ] Hover states ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö desktop
- [ ] Touch-friendly spacing ‡∏ö‡∏ô mobile

### Images & Media
- [ ] Images responsive (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà overflow)
- [ ] Art direction ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (crop ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö size)
- [ ] Video/media ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ layout ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏ô

### Accessibility
- [ ] WCAG contrast ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å breakpoint
- [ ] Focus order logical ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å size
- [ ] Screen reader order ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

---

| Output | Format | ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà |

| Figma Frames | Import ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô html-to-design MCP (`import_html` / `import_url`) | ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ import ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Figma |

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

1. **Content First**: ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å content priority ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà layout
2. **Mobile First**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö mobile ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß enhance ‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ primary = mobile)
3. **Progressive Enhancement**: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° features/content ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° screen ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏ç‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
4. **Consistent Identity**: ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å breakpoint ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô app ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
5. **Test Real Content**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ real content length ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà Lorem Ipsum
6. **Performance**: Mobile ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß ‚Äî ‡∏•‡∏î content, optimize images
7. **Fluid > Fixed**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ relative units (%, fr, auto) ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ fixed pixels
8. **Breakpoints ‚â† Devices**: ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° content ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° device ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏á

# UX Writer Skill

‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô UX Copy ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡∏¢ ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏© ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏û

## Overall Flow

```
1. Context ‚Üí 2. Voice & Tone ‚Üí 3. Write ‚Üí 4. Review & Polish ‚Üí 5. Apply (Optional)
```

1. **Context**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠, ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ, ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
2. **Voice & Tone**: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î voice/tone ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö brand + ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
3. **Write**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô copy ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏±‡∏™ ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏©
4. **Review & Polish**: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° UX Writing Principles + ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î/‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå + ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Correction Log
5. **Apply**: ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà text ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ HTML preview ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Figma (optional)

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Context

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏):

- **Screen/Feature**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô copy ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ feature ‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **User**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£? ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö tech-savviness?
- **Language**: ‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢, ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏©, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤?
- **Situation**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ? ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ì‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£?
- **Tone**: ‡∏°‡∏µ brand voice/tone ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á? (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Standard Tone)
- **Existing Design**: ‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô copy ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°?
- **Scope**: ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á element?

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ Figma URL:
```
get_screenshot(fileKey, nodeId)       ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π visual context
scan_text_nodes(nodeId)               ‚Üí ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô text ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
read_my_design()                      ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏π design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å
```

---

## Step 2: Voice & Tone

### 2.1 Standard Voice (‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ brand voice ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î:

| Attribute | ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ |
|-----------|----------|
| **‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô** | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏î‡πá‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏π‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß |
| **‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏£** | ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏´‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå |
| **‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠** | ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ |
| **‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏û** | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏©‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Ñ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô |
| **‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à** | ‡∏™‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ |

### 2.2 Tone ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå

Tone ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó ‡πÅ‡∏°‡πâ Voice ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô:

```

Body:    "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Å‡∏π‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠ ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏î ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß"
         / "All your data will be permanently deleted, including order history, favorites, and personal info. This can't be undone."
Buttons: [‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å] [‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏£]
         / [Cancel] [Delete Account Permanently]
```

### 3.2 ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ ‚Äî ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞

| ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ | ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á |
|---------|----------|----------|
| ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥ | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤" |
| ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ | ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ | "‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á" ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà" |
| ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö/‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏∞ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏° | ‡πÉ‡∏ô chatbot ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô UI ‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô | UI: "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß" / Chat: "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö" |
| ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ | ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ | "‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö" ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô" |
| ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ | ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ | "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏µ‡∏¢‡πå‡∏≠‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏•‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏™‡πå" |
| ‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ì‡∏ë‡∏¥‡∏ï | ‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô | "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πå), "‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå" (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πá‡∏õ‡πÑ‡∏ã‡∏ï‡πå) |
| ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì" ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô | "‡∏ï‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤" ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡∏ï‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì" |
| ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤" ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÜ | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" |

### 3.3 ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏© ‚Äî ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞

| ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ | ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á |
|---------|----------|----------|
| Use sentence case | Capitalize first word only | "Create new account" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "Create New Account" |
| Use contractions | ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏ä‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥ | "You're all set" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "You are all set" |
| Avoid "please" everywhere | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÜ | "Enter your email" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "Please enter your email" |
| Use "you/your" sparingly | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô | "Cart" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "Your cart" |
| Active voice | ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ passive | "We sent a code" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "A code was sent" |
| Front-load keywords | ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏Ñ | "Password must be 8+ characters" |
| No jargon | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ | "Something went wrong" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "An unexpected error occurred" |
| Oxford comma | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô list | "name, email, and password" |

## Step 4: Review & Polish

### 4.1 UX Writing Checklist

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ checklist ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ:

|---|-------|-------|
| 1 | **‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô** | ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡∏¢? |
| 2 | **‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ö** | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô? |
| 3 | **‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå** | ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? |
| 4 | **‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Tone** | Tone ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? |
| 5 | **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÇ‡∏ó‡∏©‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ** | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ß‡∏Å/‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°? |
| 6 | **‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ** | ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏Ñ, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≠, idiom? |
| 7 | **‡∏™‡∏°‡πà‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠** | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app? |
| 8 | **‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å state** | ‡∏°‡∏µ copy ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö success, error, empty, loading? |
| 9 | **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö** | text ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ô container? ‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö layout? |
| 10 | **‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å** | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à typo, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå? (‡∏î‡∏π Section 4.2 Spell & Grammar Check) |

### 4.2 Spell & Grammar Check (Thai + English)

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° ‚Äî ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î, ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î, ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î, ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Correction Log

#### ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á copy ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à copy ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma:

| ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î | ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏° ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà" ‚Üí "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠ ‡∏™‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏π‡πà" (‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô) |
| "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á" ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á" ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô | "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì" ‚Üí "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ" |
| "‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£" ‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÜ | "‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤" ‚úÖ (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô noun) ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà "‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤" ‚Üí "‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤" |

**‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏©:**

| ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î | ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å | ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ |
|-----|-----|---------|
| "Login" (as verb) | "Log in" (verb), "Login" (noun/adj) | ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å verb ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö noun |
| "Setup" (as verb) | "Set up" (verb), "Setup" (noun/adj) | ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å verb ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö noun |
| "Signin" / "Signout" | "Sign in" / "Sign out" | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô verb |
| "Its" vs "It's" | "It's" = it is, "Its" = possessive | ‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô |
| "Your" vs "You're" | "You're" = you are | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏ó‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å |
| Subject-verb disagreement | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à singular/plural | "Your settings has been saved" ‚Üí "...have been saved" |
| Double negatives | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ positive form | "Not uncommon" ‚Üí "Common" |

#### Correction Log Format

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Correction Log:

```markdown
## üìù Correction Log: [Screen/Feature Name]

| # | ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á (Location) | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏° (Original) | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ (Corrected) | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î (Error Type) | ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏• (Reason) |
|---|---------------------|------------------------|---------------------------|---------------------------|-----------------|
| 1 | Login button | "‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô" | "‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö" | ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå ‚Üí ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ | ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° terminology table: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ "‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö" ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô "‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô" |
| 2 | Error message | "‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà" | "‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á" | ‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î + ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ì‡∏≤" ‚Üí "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤" (‡∏ì ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß), ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á" ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô |
| 3 | Page title | "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå" | "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏û‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå" | ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î | "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó" ‚Üí "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï" (‡∏õ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà ‡∏û, ‡∏ï ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà ‡∏ó) |
| 4 | Success toast | "Your settings has been saved succesfully." | "Your settings have been saved." | Grammar + Spelling | "has" ‚Üí "have" (plural subject), "succesfully" ‚Üí ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å (‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö "saved") |
| 5 | Helper text | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô" | "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•" | ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå + ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤" + "‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£" ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô, "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•‡πå" ‚Üí "‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•", "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô |

### ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ (Summary)
- ‚úÖ ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î: X ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
- ‚ùå ‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î: Y ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- üî§ ‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î (Spelling): N ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- üìù ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå (Grammar): N ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- üîÑ ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î (Transliteration): N ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- üìñ Terminology ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á: N ‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- ‚ú® ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß: N ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°
```

#### ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à copy ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Figma design:

```
1. scan_text_nodes(nodeId)                ‚Üí ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á text ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å text node ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏ô

     { nodeId: "error-text-id", text: "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß" },
     ...
   ])

     nodeId: "screen-id",
     annotations: [
       { nodeId: "fixed-text-id", labelMarkdown: "**Spell Check**\n'‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ó' ‚Üí '‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï'\n‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏®‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ó‡πå‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ì‡∏ë‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏Ø" }
```

### 4.3 Terminology Consistency Table

‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á terminology ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á app ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô:

```markdown
| Concept | ‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ | English | ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ |
|---------|-----|---------|---------|
| Sign in | ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏π‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö | Sign in | ‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô, Login, Log in |
| Sign up | ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å | Create account | ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ö‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô, Register, Sign up |
| Sign out | ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö | Sign out | ‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏ó‡πå, Logout |
| Password | ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô | Password | ‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏™‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏î |
| Delete | ‡∏•‡∏ö | Delete | ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å, Remove (‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô remove from list) |
| Save | ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å | Save | ‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏ü |
| Cancel | ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å | Cancel | ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ |
| Settings | ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ | Settings | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤) |
| Search | ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ | Search | ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏£‡πå‡∏ä, ‡∏´‡∏≤ |
```

‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°/‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ terminology table ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£

### 4.4 Character Count Guidelines

‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ copy ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö:

| Element | Max (‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢) | Max (EN) | ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏ |
|---------|-----------|----------|----------|
| Button | 12 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 20 characters | ‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏î‡∏µ |
| Tab label | 8 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 12 characters | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î |
| Nav item | 8 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 12 characters | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£ 2 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î |
| Toast/Snackbar | 40 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 60 characters | ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏ß |
| Title | 20 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 30 characters | 1 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î |
| Body text | ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö | ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö | Line length 45-75 chars |
| Tooltip | 30 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 50 characters | ‡∏™‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î |
| Error (inline) | 40 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ | 60 characters | ‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏µ 2 ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏î |

## Step 5: Apply ‚Äî ‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà Text ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Design (Optional)

### Option A: Apply ‡∏•‡∏á HTML Preview File

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ HTML preview (.html) ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà/‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ copy:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Read tool ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå `.html`
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Edit tool ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ text content ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå HTML
- User refresh browser ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ

### Option B: Apply ‡∏•‡∏á Figma

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ Figma design ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà copy:

### 5.1 ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Text ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà

```

```

### 5.2 ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ Text

```

set_multiple_text_contents(parentId, [               ‚Üí ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ nodes ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
  { nodeId: "title-id", text: "‡∏ï‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì" },
  { nodeId: "subtitle-id", text: "3 ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£" },
  { nodeId: "button-id", text: "‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ã‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠" }

```

### 5.3 Annotate

‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà annotation ‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ copy decisions:
```
set_multiple_annotations({
  nodeId: "screen-id",
  annotations: [
    { nodeId: "error-text-id", labelMarkdown: "**Error copy**\n‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£: [‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î] + [‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ]\nTone: ‡∏™‡∏á‡∏ö, ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠" },
    { nodeId: "cta-id", labelMarkdown: "**CTA**\n‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏¢‡∏≤\nMax 12 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏£ (TH)" }
  ]
})
```

## ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç

4. **‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö**: "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß" ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà "Data saved successfully to database"

# Jira Requirement Analysis Skill

‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå Requirements ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Jira Card ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á BA ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏° UI Design Scope

---

## Trigger

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ skill ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠:
- ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏Å Jira issue key (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô PROJ-123)
- ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏û‡πå "jira", "analyse req", "‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå requirement", "card analysis", "BA req", "jira card"
- ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ paste requirement text ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å BA/PM

---

## Step 1: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Jira Card

### ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ Jira MCP (‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å tools ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà available)

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏° issue key ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:

```
jira_get(
  path: "/rest/api/3/issue/{issueKey}",
  jq: "{key: key, summary: fields.summary, description: fields.description, status: fields.status.name, priority: fields.priority.name, labels: fields.labels, issueType: fields.issuetype.name}"
)
```

‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á comments ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢:
```
jira_get(
  path: "/rest/api/3/issue/{issueKey}/comment",
  jq: "comments[*].{author: author.displayName, body: body, created: created}",
  queryParams: { maxResults: "10" }
)
```

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ subtasks:
```
jira_get(
  path: "/rest/api/3/search/jql",
  queryParams: { jql: "parent={issueKey}", maxResults: "20" },
  jq: "issues[*].{key: key, summary: fields.summary, status: fields.status.name}"
)
```

### ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ Jira MCP

‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ:
> "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤ paste ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤ requirement ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Jira card ‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö (summary, description, acceptance criteria)"

---

## Step 2: ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå Requirements

‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Jira card ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô:

### 2.1 User Stories

‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å requirement ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô User Stories format:
```
As a [user type], I want to [action], so that [benefit]
```

### 2.2 Acceptance Criteria

‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á acceptance criteria (AC) ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô checklist:
- AC ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô card
- AC ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà implied ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å description
- AC ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏õ (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°)

### 2.3 Business Rules

‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏é‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞:
- Validation rules (format, length, required fields)
- Permission/role ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- Limits/quotas
- Dependencies ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô

### 2.4 Edge Cases

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏ edge cases ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö:
| Case | Description | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ UI ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö? |
|------|-------------|-------------------|
| Empty State | ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà |
| Error State | API fail, validation error | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà |
| Loading State | ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà |
| Success State | ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà |
| Permission Denied | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö |
| Offline | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ internet | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö |
| Long Text | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πà |
| Max Items | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö |
| First Time User | ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å | ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö |

### 2.5 Dependencies

- Feature/screen ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- API endpoints ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
- Data models

## Step 3: ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ UI Scope

Output ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô structured summary:

### Screen List

| # | Screen Name | Description | Priority |
|---|-------------|-------------|----------|
| 1 | ... | ... | Must have |
| 2 | ... | ... | Must have |
| 3 | ... | ... | Nice to have |

### State Matrix

| Screen | Default | Filled | Error | Loading | Success | Empty |
|--------|---------|--------|-------|---------|---------|-------|
| Screen 1 | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ |
| Screen 2 | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | ‚úÖ | - | ‚úÖ | - |

### Component List

‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ component ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö:
- Navigation: tabs, back button, etc.
- Forms: input fields, dropdowns, etc.
- Actions: buttons, links, etc.
- Feedback: toast, alerts, etc.

### User Flow Summary

**Happy Path**:
1. User ‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ screen ‚Üí ...
2. User ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‚Üí ...
3. User ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô ‚Üí ...
4. ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á success ‚Üí ...

**Error Paths**:
- Validation error ‚Üí ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á inline error
- API error ‚Üí ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á error dialog
- ...

## Step 4: ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Design Approach

### Platform Pattern

‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á platform guidelines:
- **iOS**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/hig.md` ‚Äî navigation, modals, forms
- **Android**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/material-design.md` ‚Äî components, layout
- **Web**: ‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á + responsive patterns

### UX Principles ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/ux-principles.md` ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥:
- **H1 (Visibility)**: ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô status ‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î
- **H3 (User Control)**: ‡∏°‡∏µ undo/back ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î
- **H5 (Error Prevention)**: validate ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô submit
- **H9 (Error Recovery)**: error message ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô + ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ
- **Hick's Law**: ‡∏•‡∏î choices ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ screen
- **Miller's Law**: ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• 5-9 items
- (‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° context ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á requirement)

### Design Tokens ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô `references/design-tokens.md` ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏:
- Color tokens ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ (primary, error, success, etc.)
- Typography ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏° (heading, label, caption)
- Spacing pattern
- Component patterns

### Similar App/Pattern References

## Step 5: ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ Design

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user review ‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°:

> "‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö UI ‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö? ‡∏ú‡∏°‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á HTML preview ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¢"

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ user ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°:
- ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Step 1-4 ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô input ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö **figma-ui-design-spec** skill
- ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á: Screen list, State matrix, Component list, User flow, Design approach ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô requirements

## Output Format

### UI Requirements Summary

```markdown
# UI Requirements Summary

## Source
- Jira: {ISSUE_KEY} ‚Äî {Summary}
- Status: {Status}
- Priority: {Priority}

## User Stories
1. As a {user}, I want to {action}, so that {benefit}
2. ...

## Screens to Design
| # | Screen | States | Components |
|---|--------|--------|------------|
| 1 | ... | default, filled, error, loading, success | ... |
| 2 | ... | ... | ... |

## User Flow
{Happy path + error paths}

## Edge Cases
{Edge case list}

## Design Approach
- Platform: {iOS/Android/Web}
- Key UX Principles: {H1, H5, H9, ...}
- Design Tokens: {primary, error, ...}
- References: {similar apps}

## Acceptance Criteria Checklist
- [ ] AC 1
- [ ] AC 2
- ...
```
